1b1(sna tshogs): rnams
1b2(sna tshogs): ng+ge/ de/
2a1(sna tshogs): Ar+yA pra dz+nyA pAr/
2a2(sna tshogs): ra/ da /
2a3(sna tshogs): ya ga go/ bod
2b1(sna tshogs): skad du/ 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol
2b2(sna tshogs): tu phyin pa bsdud pa tshigs su bcad pa/ 'phag
2b3(sna tshogs): pa 'jam dpal la pag 'tshal lo// de nas/
3a1(sna tshogs): yang bcom ldan 'das kyis
3a2(sna tshogs): 'khor bzhi po de dag yang dag par rab du dag
3a3(sna tshogs): pabar mdzad pa'i phyir yang / shes rab kyi pha
3b1(sna tshogs): rol tu phyin pa 'di ston cing / de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dgra
3b2(sna tshogs): bka' stsol to// dga' dang gus dang dad pa'i mchog ni nyer
3b3(sna tshogs): bzhag te/ sgrib pa nyon mongs go sa la nas dri ma las 'das
3b4(sna tshogs): pa/ 'gro don mngon zhugs nges pa'i shes rab pha rol phyin/
4a1(sna tshogs): gang la dpa' rnams spyod pa de ni mnyan par gyis//
4a2(sna tshogs): 'dzam bu gling 'dir chu klung ji snyed cig 'bab cing // me tog 'bras
4a3(sna tshogs): ldan sran dang nags tsho le ba skyod byed pa// madros gnas pa'i
4a4(sna tshogs): dbang klu bdag rten gnas te// de ni klu yi bdag po de yi mthu
4b1(sna tshogs): dpal yin// rgyal ba'i nyan thos pa dag ji snyed chos ston dang // 'chang dang rigs pa
4b2(sna tshogs): dag dang ldan par brjod pa dang // mchog 'phags bde ba byed dang de yi 'bras thob pa// de
4b3(sna tshogs): dag kun kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i skyes bu'i mthu// ci phyir zhe na rgyal bas chos tshul
4b4(sna tshogs): gang bstan pa// de la mi mchog slob mor gyur pas mngon bslabs shing // mngon sum byas
4b5(sna tshogs): nas bslab pa ji bzhin byed de// sangs rgyas mthus byed rang gi stobs kyi mthus ma yin//
5a1(sna tshogs): gang la shes rab pha rol tu phyin mchog mi dmigs shing // byang chub sems
5a2(sna tshogs): dpa' mi dmigs byang chub sems mi dmigs// de skad thos nas rmongs pa med cing mi skrag pa// byang chub
5a3(sna tshogs): sems dpa' de ni bde gshegs shes rab spyod// gzugs med tshor ba med cing 'du shes sems dpa'
5a4(sna tshogs): med// de la rnam shes gnas ni rdul tsam yod pa'ang min// de chos kun la mi gnas gnas pa med par
5a5(sna tshogs): spyod// yongs su bzung med bde gshegs rnams kyi byang chub thob// ji ltar kun du rtsub bzod sbyangs shes
5b1(sna tshogs): ba yis// dmigs med phung po rnam par 'jig pa 'byung ba ltar// byang chub sems dpa' gang zhig de ltar chos shes pa// mya
5b2(sna tshogs): ngan las 'das la mi reg de ni shes rab gnas// yang 'di shes rab 'di ni gang yin su yi yin// gang las yin zhes chos
5b3(sna tshogs): 'di thams cad stong par rtog/ nye bar rtags nas zham pa med cing skrag med pa// byang chub sems dpa' de ni byang chub nye ba yin//
5b4(sna tshogs): gal te mi shes bzhin du gzugs su 'du shes shing // tshor ba sems pa rnam shes phung por spyod byed la// phung 'di stong zhes rtog
5b5(sna tshogs): na byang chub sems dpa' ni// mtshan ma la spyod skye med gnas la dad ma yin// gang zhig gzugs min tsher min 'du shes sems
5b6(sna tshogs): dpo'i min// rnam par shes la mi spyod gnas pa med par spyod// de ni spyod ces bya bar mi dmigs shes rab brtan// skye med blo
6a1(sna tshogs): ldan ting 'dzin zhi ba mchog la reg/ byang chub sems gang de ltar 'dir bdag zhir gnas pa// de ni sngon gyi de
6a2(sna tshogs): bzhin gshegs pas lung bstan yin// bdag ni mnyam par bzhag ce'am langs zhes rloms sems med// ci phyir zhe na chos kyi rang
6a3(sna tshogs): bzhin yongs shes phyir// de ltar spyod na rabade gshegs rnams kyi shes par spyod// des ni spyod med spyod pa yin par rab shes phyir/
6a4(sna tshogs): chos gang spod pa de yang dmigs par mi 'gyur te// 'di ni shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spyod pa yin// gang zhig yod pa ma yin do ni med ces
6a5(sna tshogs): bya// byis pa rnams kyis de rtags yod dang med par byed// yod dang med pa 'di gnyis med pa'i chos yin te// byang chub sems dpa' gang
6a6(sna tshogs): gos 'di shes nges par 'byung // gang 'di phung po lnga dag sgyu ma 'drar shes shing // sgyu ma gzhan dang phung po gzhan du mi byed la// sna tshogs
6b1(sna tshogs): 'du shes bral zhing nye bar zhi spod pa// de ni shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spyod pa yin// dge ba'i bshes dang ldan zhing lhag mthong ldan gyur pa// rgyal
6b2(sna tshogs): ba rnams kyi yum thos skrag par yong mi 'gyur// gang zhig sdig pa'i grogs ldan gzhan gyi dring 'jog pa// de ni snod som btang chus reg zhig pa bzhin/
6b3(sna tshogs): ci phyir 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' bya zhe na// chags pa spyod byed kun la chags pa zad par 'dod// rgyal ba rnams kyi byang chub chags med gyur la reg/
6b4(sna tshogs): des na de ni byang chub sems dpa'i ming 'thob po// ci phyir 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' che zhe na// sems can tshogs rnams mang po'i mchog tu gyur pa dang /
6b5(sna tshogs): sems can khas kyi lha rnams chen po gcod pa ste// de phyir sems dpa' chen po zhes ni rab brjod do// gtong ba che dang blo che mthu che dang // rgyal ba rnams kyi
6b6(sna tshogs): theg chen mchog zhig pa dang // go cha chen po bgos shing bdud kyi sgyu 'dul ba// de yi phyir na sems dpa' che zhes rab du brjod// dper na sgyu ma mkhan gyis
6b7(sna tshogs): gzhi mdor sprul byas te// skye bo phal chen mgo mang dbye ba gcod byed pa'i// bsad bya de dag ci 'dra de ltar byang chub sems// 'gro kun sbrul 'drar rab shes de
7a1(sna tshogs): la 'jigs pa med// gzugs dang 'du shes tshor ba dang ni sems dpa' dang // rnam par shes pa ma bcing
7a2(sna tshogs): ma grol yod pa min// de ltar byang chub la 'jug zham pa'i sems med na// 'di ni gang zag dam pa rnams kyi go cha cho ga/ ci phyir 'di ni byang chub theg chen bya zhe na/
7a3(sna tshogs): de gang zhon nas sems can thams cu zlo// theg pa 'di ni nam mkha' 'dra gzhal med te/ dga' skyid bde mngon par thob byed theg pa'i mchog/ gang zhig zhon nas
7a4(sna tshogs): phyogs su 'gro ba dmigs bu med mya ngan 'das par 'gro bar gsungs pa 'gro mi dmig/ dper na mi shi de yis 'gro rgyu med pa bzhin/ rgyu des ni mya ngan 'das zhes rab tu
7a5(sna tshogs): brjod/ byang chub sems dpa' sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byeng ba'i dmigs dus gsum dag pa ste/ gang dag de ni 'dus ma byas yin spros
7a6(sna tshogs): med de/ 'di ni shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spyod pa yin/ byang chub sems mkhas rig pa gang gi dus kyi tshe/ skye med rnam par bsam te 'di ltar spyod byed cing
7a7(sna tshogs): snying rje chen po bskyed kyang sems can 'du shes med/ 'di ni shes rab pha rol byin mchog spong ba yin/ gal te sems can 'du shes sdug bsngal 'du shes bskyed/
7b1(sna tshogs): 'gro ba rnams kyi don bya sdug bsngal spang snyam ste/ bdag dang sems can yong su rtog byang chub sems dpa' ste/ 'di ni shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spod pa yin
7b2(sna tshogs): bdag ci 'dra ba de 'drar sems can thams cad shes/ sems can thams cad ci 'dra de 'drar chos kun shes/ skye ba med dang skye ba gnyi gar mi rtog pa/ 'di ni
7b3(sna tshogs): shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spyod pa yin/ 'jig rten dag na mos min ji snyed yongs brjod pa/ kun la skye ba dang ni yang dag 'das spangs nas/ ye shesa'i cha med
7b4(sna tshogs): dam pa de las gzhal med 'tho ba/ de phyir 'di ni shes rab pha rol phyin ces bya/ byang chub sems dpa' gang zhig dogs med de ltar spong / shes rab ldan te
7b5(sna tshogs): mnyam nyid gnas par shes par bya/ chos rnams rang bzhin med par yongs su shes gyur pa/ 'di ni shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spong pa yin/ gang zhig
7b6(sna tshogs): gzugs lam gnas tshor la mi gnas shing / gang zhig 'du shes mi gnas sems pa rim gnas la/ rnam shes gang mi gnas pa chos nyid gnas pa ste/ 'di na
7b7(sna tshogs): shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spyod pa yin/ rtag dang mi rtag bode dang sdug bsngal sdug mi sdug/ bdag dang bdag med de bzhin nyid dang de bzhin stong / 'bras bu thob
8a1(sna tshogs): dang dgra bcoms la mi gnas shing / rang rgyalas dang de bzhin sangs rgyasas rim gnas/ ji ltar 'dren pa 'dus ma byas
8a2(sna tshogs): khams mi gnas shing // de bzhin 'dus ma byas la yang mi gnas gnas med spyod/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' gnas med gnas/ gnas med gnas yin 'di ni rgyal
8a3(sna tshogs): khas gnas par gsungs/ gang dag bde gshegs nyan thos 'gyur bar bya snyam dang / rang sangs rgyas dang de bzhin chos rgyal 'gyur 'dod pa/ bzod pa 'di la ma brten
8a4(sna tshogs): thob par mi nus te/ dper na pha rol tshu rol 'gro dgos mi mthong bzhin/ chos 'chad pa dang nyan dang bshad bya gang yin dang / 'bras bu thob dang rgyan rgyal de bzhin
8a5(sna tshogs): 'jig rten mgon/ mkhas pa gsal bas thob pa'i mya ngan 'das gang yin/ de kun sgyu ma lta bur de bzhin gshegs pas bstan/ gang zag bzhi po 'di dag de la mi
8a6(sna tshogs): skrag te/ rgyal sras bden la mkhas dang phyir mi ldog pa dang / dgra bcom dri ma gsal cing / so ma nyi spangs pa dang / bzhi pa dge ba'i bshes kyis yongasu zin pa'o//
8a7(sna tshogs): byang chub sems dpa' mkhas rig de ltar spyod pa ni/ dgra bcom sa lam yin rkyen rtags sa la min/ thams cad mkhyen nyid ched du sangs rgyas chos rjes slob//
8b1(sna tshogs): gang zhig slob la mi slob de slob yin/ gzugs 'phel yongasu nyams dang / yongasu bzungs phyir min/ chos rnams sna tshogs yongasu bzungs phyir mi slob par/ slob
8b2(sna tshogs): cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyang yongs 'dzin la/ des 'byung gang yin 'di ni yon tan dga' ba'i slob/ gzugs ni shes rab ma yin gzugs la shes rab med/
8b3(sna tshogs): rnam shes tshor dang sems dpa' 'di dag ni/ shes rab mi yin 'di dag la yang shes rab med/ 'di ni na mkha'i khams dang mtshungs te tha dad med/ dmigs pa
8b4(sna tshogs): rnams kyi rang bzhin de ni pha mtha' med/ sems can rang bzhin gang yin de yang pha mtha' med/ na mkha'i khams kyi rang bzhin de yang pha mtha' med/ 'jig rten
8b5(sna tshogs): mkhyen pa'i shes rab de yang pha mtha' med/ 'du shes tshu rol yin zhes 'dren pas rab tu sgrags/ 'du shes rnam par bshig nas spong ba pha rol 'gro// gang dag
8b6(sna tshogs): 'du shes bral ba 'di ni rjes thob bo// de dag pha rol phyin gnas ston pa'i bka' la gnas/ gal te ston pas kyang ni gang ga'i bye snyed kyi/ bskal par bzhugs te sems
8b7(sna tshogs): can zhes sgra yongs sgrags kyang / bzod nas dag pas sems can skye bar ga la 'gyur/ 'di ni shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spyod pa yin/ gang tsheng ni pha rol phyin pa'i rnyog 'di
9a1(sna tshogs): dang / 'thun par smra gyur de tshe sngon gyis skyes mchog gis/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus na sangs rgyas 'gyur ro// nga lung bstan par
9a2(sna tshogs): gyur ces rgyal ba de skad gsungs/ shes rab pha rol phyin pa gang la mgon spod pa/ 'di ni gang zhig gus byas 'dzin dang chub byed pa/ de la dug dang mtshon dang rgas mi
9a3(sna tshogs): tshugs/ bdud dang bdud kyi phyogs kyis glags kyang rnyed mi 'gyur/ lo las bde gshegs yongasu mya ngan 'das pa yi/ mchod rten rin chen bdun las byas shing
9a4(sna tshogs): mchod byas la/ bde bar gshegs pa'i mchod rten de dag gang ga yi/ bye ma snyed kyi bye ba phrag stong zhing bkang ste/ yongasu brtag bzung zhing rnams bye ba mtha' yas
9a5(sna tshogs): dpa na/ sems can ji snyed 'khod pa de dag thams cad kyis/ las gzhan mi byed lha yi me tog spos rab dang / byug pas dus gsum bskal pa 'am/ de bas lhag
9a6(sna tshogs): mchod la/ gang zhig gang las rnam 'dren stobs bcu 'byung 'gyur ba/ bde bar gshegs kyi yum 'di glegs bam li bros te/ 'chang zhing me tog bdug pas
9a7(sna tshogs): sti stang byed gyur na/ mchod b+ha snod nams des ni char mi phod/ rgyal ba'i shes rab pha rol phyin 'di reg sngags che/ sems can khams mang mya ngan sdug bsngal
9b1(sna tshogs): chos zhi byed/ gang dag 'das dang gang dag phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten mgon// rig sngags 'di bslab sman pa'i rgyal po bla med gyur/ gang dag phan dang snying rtser/
9b2(sna tshogs): bces par spyad spyod pa/ rig sngags 'di la bslabs nas mkhas pa byang chub reg/ 'dus byas pade dang 'dus ma byas de gang yin pa/ bde ba de kun 'di las
9b3(sna tshogs): 'byung bar rig par bya/ sa bon btab nas sa la gnas te 'gyur ba/ tshogs pa rnyed nas rnam mang gzugs dag rnam par skye/ pha rol phyin lnga byang chub yon tan ji snyed pa/
9b4(sna tshogs): de dag thams cad shes rab pha rol phyin las sku/ 'khor lo bskur rgyal lam gang nas ni rtag 'gro ba/ lam de nyid nas rin chen bdun dang dpung tshogs kan/ gang
9b5(sna tshogs): nas rgyal ba'i shes rab pha rol phyin 'di 'gro/ de nyid nas ni yon tan chos kun 'gro bar 'gyur/ rgyal bas rgyal byin dri ba yongs dris lan gsol ba/ gal te
9b6(sna tshogs): gang ga'i bye snyed sangs rgyas zhing gyur la/ de kun rgyal ba'i ring srel byur bur blta mos gyur kyang / bdag ni shes rab pha rol phyin pa 'di nyid len/ ci slad ce na sku gdung
9b7(sna tshogs): mi gus bdag ma lags/ 'on kyang shes rab yongasu sgos pas mchod par bgyi/ dper na rgyal po rten mi rim 'gro thob pa ltar/ sangs rgyas ring bsrel shes rab pa
10a1(sna tshogs): rol phyin la brten/ nor bu rin chen yon tan kun lngani ring thang med/ gab rtse gang du rtsal ba der ni phyag bgyi 'os/ de phyung
10a2(sna tshogs): gyur kyang ga brtse lani dga' bgyid te/ yon tan de dag nor bu rin chen de yi lags/ de bzhin shes rab pha rol phyin mchog yon tan gyis/ rgyal ba mya ngan 'das kyang ring bsrel mchod
10a3(sna tshogs): ba bskyes/ de ltas gang zhig rgyal ba'i yon tan 'dzin 'tshal des/ shes rab pha rol phyin blang 'di ni thar pa lags/ smin pa byin pa'i sngon du 'gro ba shes rab ste/ tshul khrims
10a4(sna tshogs): bzod pa brtson 'grus bsam gtan de bzhin no// dge chos chu dmigs na phyir yongasu 'dzin pa yin/ 'di ni chos rnams thams cad tshul gcig ston par byed/ dper na 'jam
10a5(sna tshogs): bu'i gling na shing rnams bye ba stong / rnam pa sna tshogs rnam pa du ma gzugs mang ba/ grib mar gyur pa'i grangasu brjod pa ma gtogs par/ grib ma sna tshogs med cing bye brag yod
10a6(sna tshogs): ma yin/ de bzhin rgyal ba'i pha rol phyin lnga 'di dag kyang / shes rab pha rol phyin pa'i ming nyid thob par 'gyur/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid phyir yongs su bsngos byas na/ byang
10a7(sna tshogs): chub ces byar drug po 'di kun ra cig 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' gal te rab tu mi shes bzhin// gzugs dang 'du shes tshor dang sems dpa' rnam par shes/
10b1(sna tshogs): mi rtag yongs su ston pa chos la spod pa ste/ mkhas pa nam yang chos rnams 'jig par mi byed do// gang la gzugs min tshor min 'du shes mi dmigs shing // rnam par
10b2(sna tshogs): shes pa ma yin sems dpa' mi dmigs la/ chos kun skye med stong pa'i tshul du rab shes pa/ 'di ni shes rab kyi pha rol phyin mchog spong ba yin/ la las gang gi'i klung gi bye snyed
10b3(sna tshogs): zhing rnams dang / sems can ji snyed 'khod kun dgra bcom nyid btul bas/ gang gis shes rab pha rol phyin 'di yig bris te/ sems can mchog la legs byin bson nam
10b4(sna tshogs): khyad par 'phags/ ci phyir zhe na smra mchog de dag 'dir bslabs nas/ chos rnams mtha' dag stong pa nyid du 'dir ston byed/ de thos nyan thos myur du rnam par grol
10b5(sna tshogs): bar 'gyur la reg/ rang rgyal byang chub dang ni sangs rgyas byang chub reg/ myug gu med par 'jig rten sdod 'byung yod pa med na/ de la yal 'dab me tog 'bras bu
10b6(sna tshogs): ga la 'byung byang chub sems med rgyal 'byung 'jig rten yong med na/ 'bras bu brgya byin tshangs pa nyan thos ga la 'byung / nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gang tshe 'od kyi dra ba
10b7(sna tshogs): 'gyed/ de tshe sems can las byed brtson pa de bzhin du/ mkhas pa shes phyir 'jig rten byang chub sems byung na/ ye shes kyis ni sems can yon tan chos dang ldan
11a1(sna tshogs): dper na ma dros gnas pA'i klu bdag med gyur na// 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir chu rlung 'bab par ga la 'gyur// chu rlung med na
11a2(sna tshogs): me tog 'bras bu 'byung mi 'gyur// rgya mtsho la yang rin chen gzugs meng med par 'gyur// de bzhin 'dir yang byang chub sems med bde gshegs kyi// ye shes
11a3(sna tshogs): 'jig rten 'di dag kun tu ga la 'byung // ye shes med na yon tan 'phel med byang chub med// rgya mtsho 'dra ba'i sangs rgyas chos kyang med par 'gyur// 'jig
11a4(sna tshogs): rten 'di na snang byed srog chags ji skyed pa// kun gyis snang bar bya phyir 'od rnams byung ba bas// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor 'od zer gcig phyung ches mchog ste// snang byed
11a5(sna tshogs): tshogs kyi 'od rnams kun gyis char mi phod// nyan thos tshogs rnams ji snyed sman dang tshul khrims dang // bsgom dang rab tu ldan pa'i bsod nams tshogs bskyed
11a6(sna tshogs): pa'ang // byang chub sems dpa'i rjes su yid rang sems gcig la// nyan thos tshogs kyi bsod nams phung pos char mi phod// 'das dus sngon gyi sangs rgyas skye
11a7(sna tshogs): kha khrag khrig gang // zhing mang mtha' yas bye stong dag na gang bzhugs dang // gang yang mya ngan 'das pa 'jig rten mgon po rnams// sdug bsngal zad par
11b1(sna tshogs): bya phyir rin chen chos ston pa// dang por byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed bskyed pa nas// rnam par 'dren pa rnams kyi dam chos zad kyi dus// de bar rgyal ba de
11b2(sna tshogs): dag bsod nams gang yin dang // pha rol phyin dang ldan dang sangs rgyas chos gang dang // gang yang sangs rgyas sras rnams dang ni nyan thos dang // slob dang mi slob
11b3(sna tshogs): zag bcas zag med pa// bsdus nas byang chub sems dpa' rjes su yi rang zhing // 'gro ba'i don rgyu byang chub phyir na thams cad bsngo// yongs bsngo gal te
11b4(sna tshogs): sems su 'du shes 'byung 'gyur zhing / byang chub 'du shes yongs bsngo sems ni gsum la chags// dmigs pa yod pas yongs su bsngos par tshud ma
11b5(sna tshogs): yin// gal te 'di ltar chos 'di 'gags shing zag pa dang // gang du yongs su bsngo ba de yang zad pa dang / chos kyis chos la nam yang mi sngo shes gyur na// de ltar
11b6(sna tshogs): rab tu shes par yongs su bsngos pa yin// gal te mchen mar byed na de ni bsdo ma yin// ci te mtshan pa med na byang chub bsdom yin// ji ltar dug dang 'dres
11b7(sna tshogs): pa'i kha zas bzad zag/ dkar po'i chos la dmigs pa'ang de 'drar rgyal bas gsungs/ de ltas 'di ltar yongasu bsngob bslab bya ste// ji ltar rgyal ba de dag dade/
12a1(sna tshogs): ba de mkhyen pa'i// rnam pa gang yin 'byung gang mtshan nyid gang yin la// rjes su yid rang de ltar de ltar yongs su bsngo// de
12a2(sna tshogs): ltar bsod nams byang chub yongs su bsngo byed na// dag med sangs rgyas mi spong rgyal bas gsungs pa smra// de ltar yongs bsngo dpa' bo 'jig rten dmigs can gyi// byang
12a3(sna tshogs): chub sems dpa' ji snyed thams cad zil gyis gnon/ 8/ dmus long dmigs med pa bye ba khrag khrig rnams// lam yang mi shes grong khyer 'jug par ga la 'gyur// shes rab
12a4(sna tshogs): med ni mig med pha rol phyin lnga 'dis// dmigs bu med pas byang chub reg par nus ma yin// gang tshe shes rab kyis ni rab tu zin gyur pa// de tshe mig skyed gyur cing 'di yi
12a5(sna tshogs): ming 'thob po// dper ni ri mo'i las ni yongs zin mig med pa// ji srid mig ma dris par rngan pa mi thob bzhin// gang tshe 'dus byas 'dus ma byas dang dkar nag chos//
12a6(sna tshogs): shes rab rnam par bshig na rdul tsam mi dmigs che// 'jig rten dag na shes rab pha rol phyin grangs 'gro// na mkha' gang la cung zad mi gnas de dang 'dra// sems
12a7(sna tshogs): can// sdug bsngal reg pa khrag khrig mang grol sems// sem can 'du shes yongs rtog byang chub sems dpa' ste// 'di ni shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spyod pa yin/
12b1(sna tshogs): byang chub sems dpa' gang zhig sngon chad spyod pa'i tshe// pha rol phyin 'dir smad pa mkhas pa som nyi med// thos ma thag tu de ni ston pa'i 'du shes bskyed// des ni byang chub
12b2(sna tshogs): zhi ba myur du rtogs par 'gyur// sngon sprod tshon sangs rgyas khrag khrig bkur byas kyang // rgyal ba'i shes rab pha rol phyin la ma dang na// thos nas blo chung de yis 'di ni bong byed de/
12b3(sna tshogs): spangs nas skyabs med gyur pa de ni mnar mid 'gro// de lta bas na gal te sangs rgyas ye shes mchog/ reg par 'dod na rgyal ba'i yum 'dir dad par bgyis// dper na/
12b4(sna tshogs): tshong pa rin chen gling du song nas ni// zong zad slar log lta bur gyur na mi rung ngo // gzugs kyi dag pa 'bras bu dag par rig par bya// 'bras bu gzugs dag thams cad mkhyen
12b5(sna tshogs): nyid dag par 'gyur// thams cad mkhyen nyid 'bras bu dag dang gzugs dag pa// na mkha'i khams dang mtshungs te dbyer med spyad tu med// dpa' bo gar spod shes rab pha rol
12b6(sna tshogs): phyin pa yis// khams gsum yang dag 'das las rnam par grol ba'ang min/ nyon mongs gsal bar gyur kyang skye ba ston par byed// rga dang na dang 'chi ba med kyang
12b7(sna tshogs): 'pho ston// 'gro ba 'di dag ming dang gzugs kyi 'dam la chags// rlung gi 'khor lo lta bu'i 'khor ba'i 'khor lor 'khyam// 'gro ba 'khrul pa ri dgas
13a1(sna tshogs): rgyar chung 'drar shes nas// shes rab ldan pa mkha' la bya bzhin rnam par rgyu// spyod pa yongs dag gang zhig gzug
13a2(sna tshogs): la mi spod cing // rnam shes 'du shes tshor ba sems dpar mi spod na// de ltar smod pa chags pa thams cad yongs spong zhing // chags las rnam grol bde gshegs
13a3(sna tshogs): rnams kyi shes rab spyod// de ltar spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' mkhas gsal ba// chags pa spyad nas 'gro la chags pa med par 'gro// nyi ma sgra can bza' bral
13a4(sna tshogs): lha der 'dug pa dang // me btang rtsa dang shing dang nags tshal sreg pa bzhin// chos rnams thams cad rang bzhin dag cing longs dag par/ byang chub sems dpa'
13a5(sna tshogs): shes rab pha rol phyin ltan/ byed pa po yang mi dmigs chos kun mi dmigs te// 'di ni shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spyod pa yin// rgyal ba la ni lha rgyal brgya byin gyi
13a6(sna tshogs): zhus pa// byang chub sems dpa' shes rab pa spyod pa ji ltar brtson// phung po khams la rdul tsam brtson par mi byed cing // phung por mi brtson de ni byang chub sems
13a7(sna tshogs): dpo'i brtson// gang zhig chos 'di sprul dang sgyu ma 'drar thos nas// som nyi med cing slob la phyir zhing sbor byed pa// sems can de ni ring nas zhugs reg bya// sangs
13b1(sna tshogs): rgyas bye ba khrag khrig mang la lhag byas yin// dgon pa'i lam ni dpag tshad mang por zhugs pa'i mis// gnag rdzi 'tshams kyi nags tshal phun sum tshogs mthong na/
13b2(sna tshogs): 'di dag grong dang khyer nye ba'i rtags snyam te// dbugs phyin rnyed par gyur cing chom rkun 'jig pa med// de dag byang chub yongs tshol tshe rgyal rnams kyis ni// shes rab pha rol
13b3(sna tshogs): phyin 'di mnyan pa gang thob pa// dbugs phyin rnyed par gyur cing chom rgan 'jog pa med// dgra bcom sa la ma yin rkyen rtogs sa la min// mi zhig rgya mtsho'i chu ni lta
13b4(sna tshogs): phyir 'gro ba yis// gal te shing dang nag tshal ri mthong da dung ring // ci ste rtags ma mthong na rgya mtsho chen po ni// nye bar gyur to snyam ste de la som nyi med// de ltar byang chub
13b5(sna tshogs): dam pa rab zhags rgyal ba yi// shes rab pha rol phyin pa 'di nyan rig par bya// rnam par 'dren pas mngon sum lung bstan ma gyur kyang // sangs rgyas byang chub ring
13b6(sna tshogs): por mi thogs bdag reg 'gyur// dpyid dus bzang ldong po lo ma lhags gyur na// yal gas ring po mi thogs lo 'bras me teg skran// shes rab pha rol phyin 'di
13b7(sna tshogs): su yi lag thob pa// ring por mi thogs 'dren pa rnams kyi byang chub 'thob// dper na bud med sgram gang sdug bsngal nyen gyur na// de ni de yi rtsa ba'i dus la babazhe bya/
14a1(sna tshogs): de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' rgyal ba'i shes rab nyan// dga' dang 'dun pa bskyed pa myur du byang chub reg/ shes rab
14a2(sna tshogs): pha rol phyin mchog spod tshe rnal 'byor pa// gzugs kyi 'phel ba dang ni yongs su 'grib mi mthong // gang zhig chos dang chos min chos dbyings ma mthong zhing // ma
14a3(sna tshogs): ngan 'das la mi reg de ni shes rab gnas// gang zhig 'dir spyod sangs rgyas chos rnams mi rtog ste// stobs dang rdzu 'phrul rkang pa byang chub zhi mi rtogs// rnam par
14a4(sna tshogs): mi rtog bral byin gyis brlabs kyis spong // 'di ni shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spod pa yin// smra ba'i zla ba sangs rgyas la ni rab 'byor zhes// yon tan dga' ba
14a5(sna tshogs): rnams kyi bar du gcod gang lags// ston pas bka' bstsal bar do gcod par 'gyur mang ste/ de las re zhig cung zad tsam zhig yongs su brjod// rgyal ba'i shes
14a6(sna tshogs): rab pha rol phyin 'di yig 'bri che// spobs pa tha dang rnam pa du ma 'byung 'gyur zhing // 'gro ba'i don ma byas par klog bzhin myur du yang // yongs su mnyams
14a7(sna tshogs): par 'gyur ba 'di ni bdud kyi las// 'di bshad tshe na kha cig som nyi za 'gyur te// 'dren pas 'di rin bdag gi ming yongs ma brjod// rigs dang rus kyang yod
14b1(sna tshogs): sum brjod cing // de ni mnyam par mi 'gyur srong 'gyur bdud kyi las// de ltar mi shes de dag rtsab bor nas ni// rmongs pas yal ga dag dang 'dab mtshol bar
14b2(sna tshogs): 'gyur/ glang po rnyed kyang glang po'i rjes ni tshol ba ltar// shes rab pha rol phyin thos mdo tshol de bzhin no// dper na la las ro brgya ldan pa'i
14b3(sna tshogs): zad rnyed nas/ zad mchog rnyed nas zas ngan tshol bar byed pa ltar// byang chub sems dpa' sha pha rol phyin pa 'di snyed nas/ dgra bcom pas yis byang chub
14b4(sna tshogs): chol byed de bzhin no// sti stang 'dod par 'gyur zhing rnyed pa 'dod 'gyur la// lha dang bcas pa'i sems kyis khyim 'dris byed ldan zhing // chos btang nas ni chos min
14b5(sna tshogs): bya ba spyod 'gyur// lam bor lam gol 'gro ba 'di ni bdud kyi las// gang gi tshe na 'dun cing dang gyur nas// chos kyi dam pa 'di ni nyan du song ba lags// de dag
14b6(sna tshogs): gi sin tshes smra bya bar lnga ni rig nas// dga' ba med cing yid mi bde bar gyur nas 'gro// de'i tshe bdud kyis las 'a 'gyur// de tshe gang dag gis ni dge slong mang
14b7(sna tshogs): dkrugs nas/ shes rab pa rol byin 'di 'dzin pa mi 'gyur ba'i// bar du gcod pa rnam mang gzhan yang 'byung bar 'gyur/ rin cheni rin thang med pa rnyed gyur
15a1(sna tshogs): gang dag yin// de dag dkon la dus rnams rtag tu 'tshe ba'ang mang // de bzhin rgyal ba'i shes rab pha rol
15a2(sna tshogs): phyin pa mchog/ rin chen chos kyang dkon la rtag tu 'che ba'ang mang // theg pa gsar du zhugs pa'i sems can blo chung ba// gang zhig dkon pa'i rin chen 'di ni ma
15a3(sna tshogs): rnyed pa// de la bar chad baphyir bdud ni spro bar 'gyur// phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas de dag yongs su 'dzin la sbyor// ma zhig na bar gyur la bu ni mang yod pa// de kun yid
15a4(sna tshogs): mi bde zhing de la rim 'gro byed// de bzhin phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten khams kyi sangs rgyas kyang // yum 'gyur shes rab dam pa 'di la dgongs pa mdzad// gang dag 'das
15a5(sna tshogs): dang phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten mgon gang dang // ma 'ongs dus ni 'gyur de dag 'di las 'byung // 'jig rten ston pa rgyal ba rnams kyi bskyed byed yum// sems can gzhan
15a6(sna tshogs): gyi sems kyi spyod pa ston par byed// 'jig rten de bzhin nyid dang dgra bcom de bzhin nyid// rang rgyal de bzhin nyid dang rgyal sras de bzhin nyid// cig pa nyid de dngos bral
15a7(sna tshogs): gzhin min de bzhin nyid// shes rab pha rol phyin pa de bzhin gshegs pas mkhyen// mkhas pas 'jig rten gnas sam mya ngan 'das kyang rung // chos nyid skyon med
15b1(sna tshogs): chos rnams stong pa 'di gnas to// byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin nyid 'di rjes su rtogs// de phyir de bzhin gshegs zhes sangs rgyas mtshan gsol to// shes ra
15b2(sna tshogs): pha rol phyin pa dga' tshal la rten pa// stob bcu rnam 'dren rnams kyi spyod yul 'di yin te// sems tsan sdug bsngal ngan song gsum las yongs 'don kyang //
15b3(sna tshogs): de dag nams kyang sems can 'gyur ba med// dper na seng ge ri su la rten nas 'jig med par/ ri dgas phra mo mang skrag byed cing sgra sgrog ltar// mi'i seng ge shes
15b4(sna tshogs): rab pha rol phyin brten nas// mu stegs can mang skrag byed 'jig rten sgra yang sgrogs// dper na na mkhar gnas pa'i nyi ma'i 'od zer na// sa 'di skems par byed cing gzugs
15b5(sna tshogs): kyang rab tu ston// de bzhin chos rgyal shes rab pha rol phyin rten pa// srid pa'i chu klung skems shing chos kyang rab tu ston// gzugs rnams mi mthong tshor ba dag
15b6(sna tshogs): kyang mi mthong zhing // 'du shes 'thong ba med la sems pa mi mthong zhing // gang la rnam par shes dang sems yid mthong med pa// 'di ni chos mthong ba yang de bzhin
15b7(sna tshogs): gshegs pas bstan// nam mkha' mthong zhes sems can tshig tu rab brjod pa// nam mkha' ji ltar mthong zhes don 'di rtag par gyis// de ltar chos mthong ba
16a1(sna tshogs): yang de bzhin gshegs pas bstan// mthong ba dpe gzhan gyis ni snyed par nus ma yin// gang gis de
16a2(sna tshogs): ltar mthong ba de yis chos kun mthong // rgyal po btang snyoms 'dug cing blon po kun byed ltar// sangs rgyas mdzad dang nyan thos chos rnams ji snyed pa// de dag tham
16a3(sna tshogs): cad shes rab pha rol phyin pas byed// rgyal po grong du mi 'gro yul 'khor mi 'gro bar// rang gi yul nas 'du ba thams cad sdud pa ltar// byang chub sems dpa' chos
16a4(sna tshogs): nyid gang du'ang mi 'gro la// sangs rgyas sa yi yon tan gang yin thams cad sdud// gang la bde gshegs byang chub sems dpa' dang bstan yod// shes rab pha rol
16a5(sna tshogs): phyin pa mchog la bsam spor ba// nyan thos rang rgya las gnyis shin tu 'dus byas nas// zil gyi mi gnon rgyal ba'i byang chub myur du 'thob// dper na rgya mtshor 'jug
16a6(sna tshogs): pa'i gruni chag gyur la// mi gang ro 'am rtsa 'am shing ni mi 'dzin pa// chung bus 'jig par 'gyur te ngogs su phyin mi 'gyur// gang zhig 'dzin pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol phyin par
16a7(sna tshogs): 'gyur// de ltar dang ldan dang ba thob pa gang zhig ni// shes rab pha rol phyin yum rjes su mi 'jug min// de dag thabs kyi yon tan shes rab yongs zin na// mchog
16b1(sna tshogs): tu rmad byung ba de gshegs byang chub myur du reg/ dper na la las rdza so ma btang chu bskyed na// nyams chung phyir ni myur du 'jig par rig par bya// so btang bum par chu bskyed
16b2(sna tshogs): lam du 'jig pa yi// 'jigs pa med cing bde bar khyim du phyin par 'gyur// de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' dang pa mang 'gyur kyang // shes rab rnam par nyams na
16b3(sna tshogs): myur du ma rungs 'gyur// dad pas shes rab de ni yongasu zer gyur na// sa gnyis shin tu 'das te byang chub mchog thob 'gyur// dper na bcos legs ma byas gru ni rgya
16b4(sna tshogs): mtsho'i nang // nor dang bcas shing tshor bar bcas te 'jig par 'gyur// gra de legs par bcos legs byas dang ldan gyur na// mi 'jig nor dang bcas pa ngogs su phyin
16b5(sna tshogs): par 'gyur// de ltar byang chub sems dpa' dad pas yongs bsgom kyang // shes rab med na byang chub las ni sgyur nyams 'gyur// de nyid pha rol phyin pa'i mchog ldan
16b6(sna tshogs): na// ma smas ma nyams rgyal ba'i byang chub reg par 'gyur// lo brgya nyi shu lon te rgas shing sdug bsngal mi// langs kyang bdag nyid 'gro bar nus pa ma yin te/
16b7(sna tshogs): de ni g.yas g.yon gnyis nas mi yis brten byas nas// 'gyel ba'i 'jig pa med cing bde glag 'gro bar 'gyur// de bzhin byang chub sems dpa'o shes rab stob
17a1(sna tshogs): chung ba// rab tu zhugs par gyur kyang bar du nyams par 'gyur// de nyid thabs dang shes rab mchog gis yongs
17a2(sna tshogs): zin na// mi nyams de bzhin gshegs kyi byang chub reg par 'gyur// byang chub sems dpa' dang po'i las kyi sa gnas gang // lhag pa'i bsam pas sangs rgyas mchog
17a3(sna tshogs): zhugs pa// slob ma bzang po bla ma gus ldan de dag gis// bla ma mkhas pa rnams la rtag tu brten par bya// ci phyir zhe na mkhas pa'i yon tan de las 'byung // de dag shes
17a4(sna tshogs): rab pha rol phyin pa rjes su ston// sangs rgyas chos rnams dge ba'i bshes la brten to zhes// yon tan kun gyi mchog mnga' rgyal bas de skad gsungs// sprin dang tshul
17a5(sna tshogs): khrims bzod dang de bzhin brtson 'grus dang // bsam gtan shes rab byang chub yongs su bsngo bar gyis// byang chub phung por zhen nas mchog 'dzin ma byed ces// dang
17a6(sna tshogs): po'i las dro skad bstan par bya// de ltar spyod pa legs mtsho smra ba'i zla ba rnams// 'gro ba'i skyabs dang dpung gnyen dang ni gnas yin te// brten dang blo dang gling dang yod
17a7(sna tshogs): 'dren 'don 'dod pa// gsal byed smon mtshos mchog sgrub mi 'khrugs yin// grags chen ldan rnams bya dga'ago cha gyon byed te// phung po khams dang skye mched rnams kyi
17b1(sna tshogs): go cha min/ theg pa gsum 'du shes bral zhing yongs su bzung ba yang / mi ldog g.yo ba med cing mi 'khrugs chos can yin/ de dag de 'dra'i chos dang ldan zhing spros pa
17b2(sna tshogs): med/ the rom som nyi yid gnyis bral zhing don dang ldan/ shes rab pha rol phyin pa thos nas mi nur ba// gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog cing mi ldog rig par bya// 'dren
17b3(sna tshogs): brnams kyi chos 'di zab ste mthong ba dga'// sus kyang rtogs pa med cing thob 'gyur med pa ltar// de phyir pha na mdzad rtser ldan byang chub rnyed nas 'di// sems can
17b4(sna tshogs): tshogs sus shes skem thugs khral chung bar mdzad// sems can rnams ni gnas la dga' zhing yul rnams 'dod// 'dzin la gnas shing mi mkhas blun rmong pun
17b5(sna tshogs): ba bzhin// thob par bya ba'i chos ni gnas med 'dzin med te// des na 'jig rten dag dang brtsod pa 'byung ba yin// na mkha'i khams ni shaR+Sha phyogs dang lho phyogs dang
17b6(sna tshogs): de bzhin nub kyi phyogs dang byang phyogs pa mtha' yas// steng dang 'og dang phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten rnams na'ang yod// tha dang gyur pa med cing bye brag gyur pa med/
17b7(sna tshogs): 'das pa'i de bzhin nyid gang ma byin de bzhin nyid// da ltar de bzhin nyid gang dgra bcom de bzhin nyid// chos kun de bzhin nyid gang rgyal ba'i de bzhin nyid/
18a1(sna tshogs): chos kyi de bzhin nyid 'di thams cad bye brag med// bde gshegs byang chub sems dpa' gang zhig thob 'dod
18a2(sna tshogs): pa// thabs dang ldan pas shes rab pha rol phyin la sbyor// 'dren pa'i shes rab med na thob par 'gyur ma yin// bya zhig lus che dpag tshad brgya rtsa lnga bcu par/ gyur
18a3(sna tshogs): la 'dab bshog zad de nyams rtsal yod min na// de yis sum bcu rtsa gsum gnas nas 'dzam gling 'dir// bdag nyid 'chongs der ni nyams nyes gyur pa bzhin// rgyal
18a4(sna tshogs): ba rnams kyi pha rol phyin pa lnga 'di yang // bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig mang por sgrub byas shing // smon lam mtha' yas rgya chen 'jig rten kyang // thabs med shes rab bral
18a5(sna tshogs): bas nyan thos nyid du ltung // sangs rgyas theg pa 'di la nges par 'byung 'dod gang // 'gro ba kun la sems snyoms pa ma'i 'du shes dang // phan pa'i sems dang byams
18a6(sna tshogs): ba'i yid kyis brtul bya zhing // tha ba med cing drang la tshig 'jam smra bar bya// 'jig rten mgon la gnas brtan rab 'byor yongs zhus pa// yon tan brgya mtsho'i nyon
18a7(sna tshogs): mongs ma mchis rtag brtan gsol// mthu che ba dang ji ltar slar ldog mi 'gyur ba// de ltar yon tan phyogs tsam rgyal bas lung bstan gsol// tha dang 'du shes
18b1(sna tshogs): bral zhing rigs pa ldan tshig smra// dge sbyong dag dang bram ze gzhan la rten ma byed// mkhas pa dus rnams rtag tu ngan song gsum po spangs// de dag dge bcu'i las kyi//
18b2(sna tshogs): lam la mngon par brtson// zang zing med par 'gro la chos ni rjes su ston// chos la cig tu dga' zhing rtag tu tshig 'jam ldan// 'gro 'chag nyal dang 'dug par shes bzhi
18b3(sna tshogs): rab tu ldan// gnya' shing gang tsam lta zhing 'gro la sems 'khrul med// gtsang byas gtsang ma'i gos 'chang gsum po dben zhing dag/ rnyed 'dod ma yin khyu mchog rtag
18b4(sna tshogs): tu chos 'dod pa// bdud kyi yul las 'das shing gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog/ bsam gtan bzhi la bsam gtan bsam gtan der mi gnas// grags pa 'dod pa yin khro
18b5(sna tshogs): bas sems dkris med// khyim par gyur kyang rtag tu dngos po kun ma chags// 'tsho ba'i phyir ni yangs longs spod tshol mi byed// drag shul spor sngags mi byed bud med
18b6(sna tshogs): sbyor sngags min// 'dong ba'i las can po mor 'gyur zhes ston mi byed// rab tu dben pa'i shes rab pha rol phyin mchog brtson// thabs dang rtsod dang bral zhing byams pa'i
18b7(sna tshogs): sems kyang brtan// kun mkhyen 'dod cing bstan la rtag tu gzhol sems ldan// mtha' 'khob kla klo skye ba'i yul mtha' rnam par spangs// rang gi sa la ngogs med rtag
19a1(sna tshogs): tu rib 'dra// chos phyir srog kyang 'dor zhing rnam 'byor rab tu brtson// mi ldog rnams ni 'di dag yin par shes par bya// gzugs
19a2(sna tshogs): dang tshor ba 'du shes sems pa rnam shes rnams// za ba ste rang bzhin mtshan ma med cing rab zhi ba// dper na mda' yis rgya mtsho'i gting thug tshol ba ltar// shes rab kyis
19a3(sna tshogs): ni yongs rtags phung po'i gting mi rnyed// byang chub sems dpa' gang zhig de ltar zab gyur cing // byed pa don dam chags med gang la phung po dang // khams dang skye mched
19a4(sna tshogs): yod min chos 'di rtogs pa de'i// bsod nams yang dag 'grub pa de las ci zhig yod// dper na 'dod chags chos las spong pa'i skyes bu zhig/ bud med dus btab
19a5(sna tshogs): de dang ma phrad de yi ni// nyin cig sems kyi rnam rtog spyod pa ji snyed pa// de snyed bskal pa'i byang chub sems dpas thob par 'gyur// byang chub sems dpa' gang zhig
19a6(sna tshogs): bskal mang byed stong du// dgra bcom rang brgyal sbyin byed tshul khrims bsrung byed kyang // gang zhig shes rab pha rol phyin mchog ldan pa'i chos// brjod pa'i legs pa
19a7(sna tshogs): sprin dang tshul khrims char mi phod// byang chub sems dpa' gang zhig shes rab mchog sgoms te// de las langs nas gos pa med pa'i chos spyod cing // de yang 'gro ba
19b1(sna tshogs): don du byang chub rgyur bsngo na// dge ba de dang mnyam pa 'jig rten gsum na med// bsod nams de dang gsog dang de bzhin stong pa dang // gsob dang ya ma rla dang snying po med
19b2(sna tshogs): shes pa// de ltar bde gshegs shes rab spang spyod na// spyod tshe bsod nams dpag tu med pa yongs su 'dzin// sangs rgyas kyis rab tu skur cing rab bstan pa'i// chos
19b3(sna tshogs): 'di thams cad brjod pa tsam du rab shes na// bskol pa bye ba khrag khrig mang por brjod byas kyang // chos kyi dbyings la zad pa med cing 'phel ba med// rgyal ba rnam kyi pha rol
19b4(sna tshogs): phyin ces bya ba gang // chos de rnams kyang ming tsam du ni yongs su bsgrags// yongs bsngo rlom sems med pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni// nyams pa med cing sangs rgyas
19b5(sna tshogs): byang chub mchog reg 'gyur// 'bru mar snying po 'bar ba phrad pa dang po yis// snying po tshigs min de med pa yang de mi tshig/ me lce phrad pa rnams snying po tshig min la// me lce
19b6(sna tshogs): tha ma med par snying po tshig min ltar// dang po'i sems kyis byang chub mchog reg ma yin la// de med par yang de la reg par nus ma yin// tha ma'i sems kyis byang chub zhi pa
19b7(sna tshogs): thob min la// de med par yang de thob nus pa ma yin no// sa bon las ni myu gu me tog 'bras bu 'byung // de yang 'gags la shing yang med pa de min ltar// de bzhi dang po
20a1(sna tshogs): sems kyang byang chub rgyu yin te// de yang 'gags byang chub med pa de ma yin// chu'i thigs pas bum pa dang po the mo'i bar// rim
20a2(sna tshogs): gyis nyung du de yongs 'gengs pa ltar// de bzhin dang po'i sems kyang byang chub mchog rgyu ste// rim gyis dkar po'i yon tan rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'gyur// stong pa mtshan ma
20a3(sna tshogs): med par chos spyod cing // mya ngan 'das la mi reg mar mi spyod pa// dper na mnyam pa mkhas pa phar 'gro tshur 'gro yang // mtha' gnyis mi gnas rgya mtshor gnas pa med pa
20a4(sna tshogs): bzhin// de ltar spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam bdag/ stobs bcus lung bstan byang chub rag 'gyur rlom sems med// 'di la ci yang med ces byang chub
20a5(sna tshogs): skrag pa med// de ltar spyod pa bde gshegs shes rab spod pa yin/ 'jig rten dgon pa'i lam dang mu ge'i nang bcas par// mthong nas skrag pa med cing de nas go
20a6(sna tshogs): gyon te// phyi ma'i mu mthar rtag tu brtson zhing rab shes naso// yongs su skyo ba'i blo ni rdul tsam bskyed mi byed// byang chub sems dpa' rgyal ba'i shes rab sbyin byed cing
20a7(sna tshogs): phung po 'di dag gdod nas stong zhing skye med shes// mnyam par ma gzhag sems can khams la snying rjer 'jug/ bar skabs der yang sangs rgyas bcom chos la yongs
20b1(sna tshogs): mi mnyams// dper na skyes bu mkhas pa yon tan kun ldan zhing // stobs ldan mi thub brtson byas sgyu rtsal chog shes pa// 'phongs dang bzo gnas mang po'i pha rol
20b2(sna tshogs): byin gyur cing // sgyub grub shes 'gre don rab tu 'dod pa zhig/ pa dang ma dang chung mar bcas pa yongs bsdus nas// dgra byed mang po dgon pa'i lam du phyin pa dang /
20b3(sna tshogs): de'i dpa' zhing brtul por skyes bu pha rol phyiran gyur cing // de'i raba'i zhid rtul bod skyes bu mang sprul te// bde bar song zhing phyir yang khyim du 'ong ba ltar// de bzhin de che byang
20b4(sna tshogs): chub sems dpa' mkhas pa yang // sems can mkham kun tu snying rje chen po yi se// / bdud bzhi dag dang sa gnyis las kyang rab 'das nas// ting 'dzin mchog la
20b5(sna tshogs): gnas shing byang chub reg mi byed// mkha' la rlung rten de la chu yi phung po rten// de la sa chen 'di rten de la 'gro ba rten// sems can las la spyod pa'i rgyu ni de 'dra ste//
20b6(sna tshogs): nam mkha' gang la gnas yin don 'di bsam par gyis// de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' stong pa nyid gnas pa/ 'gro la sems can shes pa'i smon lam brtan can gyi/
20b7(sna tshogs): bya ba rnam pa sna tshogs ston byed cing // mya ngan 'das la mi reg stong par gnas shing zhi// gang gi chen byang chub sems dpa' mkhas gsal ba// stong pazhi pa'i ting
21a1(sna tshogs): 'dzin dpa pa'idi bskyong pa// rabaskabs de ni pa can sa btu ba rnaMs mi byes/ mtshan pa med par ga
21a2(sna tshogs): shing zhi la rab zhi spyod// bar sdang phur ba'i bya la gnas yod pa yin ste// de la gnas pa ma yin sa la ltung mi 'gyur// de ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnam thar skor
21a3(sna tshogs): spyod pa/ mya ngan 'das la mi reg mtshan par spyod ma yin// dper na 'phongs brlabs skyes bus gnam du mdo' 'bangs te// mnga' gzhan dag ni phyi zhin rgyud par yod
21a4(sna tshogs): botags nas// snga pa'i mnga' des la ltung ba'i skabs mi byed// mi de 'dod na mda' des la ldang bar 'gyur// de ltar shes rab pha rol phyin pa mchog spyod pa// shes
21a5(sna tshogs): rab zabs stobs rdzu 'phrul gyis ni spyod dge/ de dag dge ba'i rtsa ba ji srid ma rtogs pa// de srid stong nyid dam pa thob mi byed// dper na dge slong rdzu 'phrul stobs
21a6(sna tshogs): mchog ldan pa zhig/ na mkha'i gnas te gcig char chos 'phrul rnam par 'phrul// 'gro dang 'chag pa dang ni nyal dang 'dug pa ston// de ni skyo ba med cing de la dub pa med/
21a7(sna tshogs): de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' mkhas pa ston gnas shing // ye shes rdzu 'phrul pa rol sor la gnas pa med// 'gro ba dag la bya ba rnam pa mtha' yas ston/
21b1(sna tshogs): skal pa bye bar skyo ba med cing dub pa med// dper na mi 'ga' g.yang sa chen por 'dug byed cing // lag pa gnyis gas gdugs gnyis 'dzin cing na mkha' la// 'tshong
21b2(sna tshogs): bar byed cing g.yang sa chen por lus bor nas// ltung bar mi 'gyur ji srid der ni 'gro bar 'gyur// de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' mkhas pa snying rjer gnas/
21b3(sna tshogs): thabs dang shes rab gnyis kyi gdugs ni yongs bzung ste// chos rnams stong pa mtshan med smon pa med rtog cing // mya ngan 'das la reg pa med la chos kyang
21b4(sna tshogs): mthong // dper na mi zhig rin chen gling song ste// rin chen rnyed nas phyir yang khyim du 'ong 'gyur ba// der ni ded dpon 'ba' zhig bde bar 'tsho byed cing // gnyen
21b5(sna tshogs): gshes tshogs yid mi bder 'jog pa min pa ltar// de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' stong nyid rin chen gyi// gling du song ste bsam gtan dbang po stobs thob pa//
21b6(sna tshogs): mya ngan 'das la reg pa 'ba' zhig mngon dga' zhing // sems can sdug bsngal yid tu 'jog par 'gyur ma yin// dper na don gnyer tshong pa rgyas shes bya ba'i phyir/
21b7(sna tshogs): bor gyi grong khyer grong rdal grong gang yin par 'gro// der yang mi gnas rin chen glong du'ang mi gnas la// rig pa khyim du mi gnas lam la mkhas par 'gyur/
22a1(sna tshogs): de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' gsal te nyen thos dang// rang rgyal rnam kyi shes pa rnam grol kun la mkhas
22a2(sna tshogs): de la mi gnas sangs rgyas ye shes gnas ma yin// 'dus ma byas la mi gnas lam gyi tshul shes min// gang tshe 'gro la byams pa rjes su 'brel byas nas/ ting
22a3(sna tshogs): 'dzin stong pa mtshan med spon pa med spyod pa/ de ni mya ngan 'das pa thob par 'gyur zhes 'am// 'dus byed yin par gdags nus de ni gnas med do// dper na sprul
22a4(sna tshogs): pa'i mi lus mi snang ma yin zhing // de ni ming gis kyang ni gdags par nus pa ltar// de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' rnam thor sgo spyod pa// de ni ming gis kyang na
22a5(sna tshogs): gdags par nus pa yin// gal te spyod pa dang ni dbang po yongs dris la// byang chub sems dpa' stong pa mtshan ma med pa'i chos// yongs su mi ston phyir
22a6(sna tshogs): mi ltos pas yo chos// mi 'chad do ni lung ma bstan pa yi ni rig bya// dgra bcoms dang rkyen gyi sangs rgyas ye shes dang // khams gsum dag la rmi lam
22a7(sna tshogs): na yang mi 'dod cing / sangs rgyas rnams mthong 'gro la chos kyang ston byed pa// de ni mi ldog lung bstan yin par rig par bya// rmi lam ni ni sems can
22b1(sna tshogs): ma gnas pathob sa kyi gang yang na song rgyan gapor sngon lam 'dengs// bden pa'i gyis 'dabs kyis seM 'i rlung chen// rnan ma ldog pa
22b2(sna tshogs): bstan yi par rig par bya// mi'i 'jig rten 'byung ba'i gdon dang na dmang ba// phan dang snying brtser ldan pa'i bden pa'i byin gyis zhe// 'on kyang rlom
22b3(sna tshogs): sems med cing nga rgyal skyod med pa// de ni mi ldog lung bstan yin par rig par bya// ci ste de ni bden pa'i byin rlabs sna tshogs dang // 'byor pas bdag lung
22b4(sna tshogs): bstan snyam rlom sems 'byung ba'am// gal te byang chub sems dpa' gzhan gyis lung bstan brlom// rlom sems gnas pa de ni blo chung shes par bya//
22b5(sna tshogs): ming gi gzhi las bdud ni nye bar 'ongs gyur nas// 'di skad smras te 'di ni khyod dang pha ma dang // khyod kyis bdun mes rgyud kyi bar gyi ming yin zhing // gang tshe
22b6(sna tshogs): khyod ni sangs rgyas 'gyur ba'i 'di yin// sbyangs sdom rnal 'byor ldan pa ci 'dra 'byung 'gyur la// khyod sngon yon tan tshul yang 'dra'o zhes brjod de// de
22b7(sna tshogs): skad gang thos rlom sems byang chub sems dpa'i ni// bdud kyis yongs su slang shing blo chung rig par bya// rab tu dben pa'i grong dang grong khyer ri sul dang /
23a1(sna tshogs): dgon pa dben pa'i gnas khrod rab tu rten byed cing // bdag bstod gzhan la spod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni//
23a2(sna tshogs): bdud kyis yongasu blang zhing blo chung rig par bya// rtag tu grong dang yul 'khyer grong rdal gnas byed kyang // sems can smin byed byang chub brtson pa ma gtogs pa// 'di ni
23a3(sna tshogs): dgra bcom rang rgyal 'dod pa gzhan mi bskyed// 'di ni bde bar gshegs pa'i sras kyis dben par gsungs// gang zhig dpag tshad lnga brgya yod pa'i ri'i sul// sprul
23a4(sna tshogs): gyis gang bar lo mang bye bar gnas byed kyang // dben pa 'di mi shes pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de// lhag pa'i nga rgyal rnyed nas 'dre bar gnas pa yin// byang chub
23a5(sna tshogs): sems dpa' 'gro ba'i don brtson bsam gtan dang // stobs dang dbang po rnam thar ting 'dzin thob de la// 'di ni dgon dben spyod pa min snyam brnyes byed pa// de ni
23a6(sna tshogs): bdud kyis spyod yul gnas zhes rgyal ba sa gsungs// gang zhig grong ngam 'on te dgon par gnas kyang rung // theg pa gnyis kyi sems bral byang chub mchog nges na/
23a7(sna tshogs): 'di ni 'gro don zhugs pa rnams kyi dben pa ste// byang chub sems dpa' drod nyo ma de ni bdag nyid nyams// de lta bas na byang chub dam pa tshol ba yi// bsam pa
23b1(sna tshogs): drag ldan mkhas pas nga rgyal nges bcom ste// nad pa'i tshogs kyi gse phyir sman pa bsten pa ltar// g.yel ba med par dge ba'i bshes gnyen brtan par bya//
23b2(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas byang chub mchog zhugs byang chub sems dpa' dag/ pha rol phyin dang bcas ste dge ba'i bshes la brten// de dag rjesu ston byed 'di ni sgrub pa'i sa/
23b3(sna tshogs): rgyu rnams gnyis kyis sangs rgyas byang chub myur du rtogs// rgyal ba 'das dang ma byon gang bzhugs pa// kun lam pha rol phyin pa 'di yin gzhan ma yin// pha rol
23b4(sna tshogs): byang chub mchog la zhugs rnams kyis gsal dang // smon dang snang dang ston mchog yin zhes bshad// ji ltar shes rab pha rol phyin 'di mtshan nyid stong // chos 'di
23b5(sna tshogs): thams cad mtshan nyid de dang 'drar shes shing // chos rnams stong zhing mtshan ma med par rab shes nas// de ltar spyod pa bde gshegs shes rab spyod pa yin// sems
23b6(sna tshogs): can yongs su rtog pas zas la 'dod byed cing // 'khor bar chags pa'i yid dang ldan rnams brtag tu 'khor// bdag dang bdag gi chos gnyis yang dag min stong ste/
23b7(sna tshogs): byis pa bdag nyid kyis ni mkha' la 'dud pabor// dper na dog pa'i 'du shes kyis ni dug langs gca dug de long du song ba med kyang rgyal bar 'gyur/ de bzhin
24a1(sna tshogs): byis pa bdag dang bdag gir khas len pa// bdag der 'du shes yang dag mi rtag skye zhing 'chi// ji ltar 'dzin pade
24a2(sna tshogs): ltar kun nas nyon mongs sten// bdag dang bdag gir mi dmigs rnam par byang bar gsung // 'di la gang yang nyon mongs rnam dag 'gyur ba med// byang chub sem
24a3(sna tshogs): dpa' shes rab pa ralo phyin pa rtogs// 'dzam bu'i gling na sems can ji snyed ma lus pa// de dag thams cad byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed nas// lo stong byed
24a4(sna tshogs): mang po sbyin pa byin byas la// kun kyang 'gro ba don phyir byang chub rgyur bsngo yang // gang zhig shes rab pha rol phyin pa la mngon brtson pa// tha na nyi ma gcig gi rjes
24a5(sna tshogs): su 'thun byed na// de la sbyin pa'i phung pos bsod nams char me phod// de phyir g.yel med rtag tu shes rab 'jug par bya// shes rab pha rol phyin mchog spyod
24a6(sna tshogs): pa'i rnal 'byor pa// snying rje chen po bskyed bcing sems can 'du shes med// de tshe mkhas pa 'gro ba kun gyi sprin gnas gyur// rtag tu yul 'khor bsod snyom
24a7(sna tshogs): don yang yongasu spyod// byang chub sems dpa' gang 'dir yun ring 'brel ba yis// lha mi ngan song gsum gyi sems can sgrol ba'i phyir// lam yang pha rol
24b1(sna tshogs): sems can khams la ston 'dod pa// nyin can shes rab pha rol byin la brtson par bya// mi zhig sngan chad ma rnyed pa yi rin chen mchog/ dus gzhan zhig
24b2(sna tshogs): nas rnyed par 'gyur de dga' ba las// rnyed ma thag tu bag med gyur ste sbyor na ni// sbyor bas rin chen mngon 'dod rtag tu sdug bsngal lo// de ltar byang chub mchog
24b3(sna tshogs): zhugs rin chen lta bu yi// shes rab pha rol phyin la rnal 'byor dor mi bya// rin chen rnyed nas blangs te rab tu brtson dkris nas// myur du 'gro bar byed pa zhi
24b4(sna tshogs): bar 'gyur ba bzhin// nyi ma sprin dang bral ba'i 'od zer 'dra ba can// mun nag thibs pa'i mun pa thams cad 'joms 'char ba/ srin bu me khyer srog chag
24b5(sna tshogs): 'byung po thams cad dang // skar ma'i tshogs dang zla ba'i 'od kun zil gyi gnon// de bzhin byang chub sem dpa' shes rab pha rol phyin// mchog spyod stong dar
24b6(sna tshogs): pa ni mtshan ma med spyod pa// mkhas pas lta ba'i thib po btsom nas 'gro kun dang // dgra bcom rang rgyal byang chub sems mang zil gyis gnon// dper
24b7(sna tshogs): na rgyal po'i bu zhig nor gtong don 'dod pa// kun gyi gtso bor gyur te mngon par 'gro bya'os// 'di ni dalta na yang sem can mang dga' byed// thabs thobs
25a1(sna tshogs): gyur te rgyal srid gnam na smos ci dgos// de ltar shes rab spyod mkhas byang chub sems dpa' yang // bdud
25a2(sna tshogs): tsa sbyin par byed cing lha dang mi rnams dga'// 'di ni da lta na yang sems can mang phan brtson// chos kyi rgyal por gnas par gyur na smos ci dgos// de yi tshe
25a3(sna tshogs): na bdud ni zug rngu ldang bar 'gyur// mya ngan nyams thag sdug bsngal yid mi bde nyams chung // ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' 'di yid nur 'gyur zhes//
25a4(sna tshogs): 'jig pa stan phyir phyog rnams sregs cing skar mda' stong // gang tshe mkhas pa de dag bsam pa rab ldan zhing // nyin mtshan shes rab pha rol phyin pa mchog
25a5(sna tshogs): don lta// de tshe lus sems dag ni mkhas 'gro bya ltar smra// nag po'i rtsa lag rnams kyis glags rnyed ga la 'gyur// gang tshe byang chub sems dpa'
25a6(sna tshogs): 'theb dang brtson gyur cing // phan tshun mi 'thur khros pa'i sems dang ldan gyur pa// de che bdud ni mchog tu dga' zhing nyams bder 'gyur// de gnyis rgyal
25a7(sna tshogs): ba'i ye shes las ni rang 'gyur snyam// de gnyis ring du 'gyur zhing sha za 'dra bar 'gyur// gnyis ga'ang rang gi dam bcas nyams par byed par 'gyur// sngang
25b1(sna tshogs): zhing bzod dang bral la byang chub ga la yod// de tshe bdud rnams phyogs dang bcas te dga' bar 'gyur// lung bstan ma tho bas byang chub sems dpa' gang zhig gis//
25b2(sna tshogs): lung bstan thob la sems rgyu rtsod pa rtsom byed na// zab skyon ldan sems kyi ska cig ji snyed pa// de snyed skal pa bzhi nas go cha bgo bgos so// sangs rgyas bzod pa'i
25b3(sna tshogs): pha rol phyin pas byang chub reg/ sems 'di bzang po min snyam pa dran pa bskyed byed cing // so sor 'chags par byed cing phyis kyang sdom byed la// dga' bar mi
25b4(sna tshogs): byed 'di ni sangs rgyas chos rjes slob// gang zhig slob tshe bslab pa gang yang mkhas mi len// slob pa po dang bslab pa'i chos rnams mi dmigs shing // slab dang /
25b5(sna tshogs): slob pa ma yin 'di gnyis mi rtog pa// de ltar gang slob de ni sangs rgyas chos 'dir slob// sems dpa' gang zhig de ni lha'i slab 'di shes// de ni bzhin yang
25b6(sna tshogs): bslab nyams tshul khrims 'tshal mi 'gyur// de ni sangs rgyas chos brnyes bya phyir 'di la bsngob// de ni bsla ba lhag bsgrub la mkhas te dmigs pa med// mkhas
25b7(sna tshogs): ba'od byed rnams kyi shes rab de ltar slob// dge ba ma yin sems cig tsam yang skyed mi byed// nyim mkha' la 'gro ba'i zer gyis zil gnon pa'o// mdun gyi bar snang
26a1(sna tshogs): li ni mun pa mi gnas bzhin// shes rab pha rol phyin la bslab par byas rnams kyi// pha rol phyin pa thams cad
26a2(sna tshogs): 'dir ni 'dus par 'gyur// 'jig tshogs lta bar lta ba drug bcu gnyis 'dus ltar// de bzhin pha rol phyin par 'di dag 'dus par gsungs// dper na srog gi dbang po
26a3(sna tshogs): 'gags na dbang po gzhan// gang dag ji snyed yod pa thams cad 'gag par 'gyur// de ltar shes rab spyod pa mkhas pa mchog rnams kyi// pha rol phyin pa thams cad
26a4(sna tshogs): 'di rin 'dus par gsungs// byang chub sems mkhas nyan thos yon tan gang dag dang // de bzhin rang rgyal yon tan kun la slob byed cing // de dag de la mi gnas 'dod
26a5(sna tshogs): ba mi bskyed to// 'di ni bdag gis bslab bya yin snyam de byi ba slob// mi ldog byang chub mchog la rab tu zhugs pa yi// sems bskyed pa la bsam pa thag pas yid rang ba/
26a6(sna tshogs): stong gsum ri rab srang la gzhal bas tshad bzung rung // rje su yid rang dge ba de ni de ltar min// dge ba don gnyer phan 'dod sems can ji snyed pa// kun gyi bsod nams
26a7(sna tshogs): phung po la yang yid rang 'gyur// de phyir de dag rgyal ba'i yon tan thob gyur nas// sdug bsngal zad par bya phyir 'jig rten chos sbyin byed// byang chub sems gang
26a8(sna tshogs): dang /
26b1(sna tshogs): zhig mi rtog chos rnams kun// stong dang mtshan ma med dang spros med yongs shes pa// de na shes rab gnyis kyis ni byang chub chol mi byed// rnal 'byor pa de shes rab pa
26b2(sna tshogs): pha rol phyin mchog brtson// nam mkha'i khams de dang ni nam mkha' der 'gal ba// yod pa ma yin gis kyang ni de ma thob// de bzhin shes rab spyod mkhas byang chub sems
26b3(sna tshogs): dpa' yang // nam mkha' lta bu yin te nye bar zhi spyod pa// skye bo'i dbus na sgyu ma'i skyes bu 'di snyam du// skye bo 'di mgu bya snyam mi sems de yang byed// rdzu 'phrul sna tshog
26b4(sna tshogs): rab tu ston par byed mthong yang // de la lus med sems med ming yang yod ma yin// de bzhin shes rab spyod mkhas nam yang 'di snyam du// byang chub rtogs nas
26b5(sna tshogs): 'gro ba yongasu sgrol mi snyems// skye ba sna tshogs dang ni bya ba mang ldan pa// sgyu ma lta bur ston kyang rnam par mi rtog spyod// dper na sangs rgyas sprul pa sangs rgyas mdzad
26b6(sna tshogs): pa byed// byed pa de la dregs pa cung zad skye mi 'gyur// de bzhin shes rab spyong mkhas byang chub sems dpa' yang // sprul pa sgyu ma bzhin du bya ba thams cad ston//
26b7(sna tshogs): shing mkhan bzo bo mkhas pas skyes pa bud med dang // 'dra ba'i bzo byas de yang bya ba thams cad byed// de bzhin shes rab spyod mkhas byang chub sems dpa' yang
27a1(sna tshogs): @rnam par mi tog ye shes bya ba thams cad byed// de ltar spyod mkhas rnams la lha tshogs mang po dag/
27a2(sna tshogs): thal mo sbyar ba btud nas phyag kyang 'tshal bar byed// phyog bcu'i 'jig rten khams kyi sangs rgyas ji snyed pa'ang // yon tan bsngags pa'i phreng ba yongasu brjod par mdzad/
27a3(sna tshogs): gang ga'i klung mnyam zhing na sems can ji snyed pa// de kun yongasu brtag bzung ste bdud gyur la// baspu nyag re las kyang de snyed sprul byas kyang // de dag kun gyis
27a4(sna tshogs): mkhas la bar chad bya mi nus/ rgyu rnams bzhi yis byang chub sems po khas stobs ldan// bdud bzhis thub par dka' zhing skyong par mi nus te// stong par gnas dang
27a5(sna tshogs): sems can yongasu mi gtong dang // ji snyed smras bzhin byed dang bde gshegs byin brlabs can// de bzhin gshegs yum shes rab pha rol phyin pa 'di// 'chad tshe byang
27a6(sna tshogs): chub sems dpa' gang zhig mos byed cing // bsam pa zag pas sgrub pa mngon par brtson byed na// des ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la zhugs rig bya// chos dbyings
27a7(sna tshogs): de bzhin nyid la gnas par mi 'gyur zhing // dper na bar snang sprin bzhin gnas pa med pa gnas// rig sngags 'chang ba gnas med mkha' rgyu gnas 'dod pa/
27b1(sna tshogs): sngags mthus dus min me tog ldan zhing byin gyis rlob// de ltar spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' mkhas gsal ba// rtogs par byed dang sangs rgyas chos rnams dmigs
27b2(sna tshogs): mi 'gyur// 'chad par byed dang chos 'dod lta bar byed mi dmigs// 'di ni zhi 'dod yon tan dga' ba'i gnas ma yin// dgra bcom rnam thar de bzhin gshegs kyi ma gtogs
27b3(sna tshogs): par// gnas pa 'di ni nyan thos rang rgyal bcas pa yi// gnas pa zhi ba'i ting 'dzin rab zhi bde ldan pa// ji snyed kun gyi mchog dang gong na med pa yin// 'dab chags
27b4(sna tshogs): mkha' la gnas kyang ltung bar 'gyur ma yin// nya ni chu la gnas kyang 'tshub sa te 'chi ba med// de ltar byang chub sems dpa' bsam gtan stobs dag gi// pha rol
27b5(sna tshogs): son pa stong gnas mya ngan 'da' mi 'gyur// sems can kun gyis yon tan mchog tu 'gro ba dang // sangs rgyas ye shes mchog tu rmad byung mchog reg dang // chos kyi
27b6(sna tshogs): sbyin pa rab mchog dam pa sbyin 'dod gang / phan mdzad rnams kyis gnas mchog 'di la rtan par gyis// bslab pa 'di ni 'dren pas bslab pa yongs brjod pa// bas
27b7(sna tshogs): ji snyed kun gyi mchog dang gong na med// mkhas pa gang zhig slab kun pha rol 'gro 'dod pas// sangs rgyas bslab pa shes rab pha rol phyin 'dir spobs/
28a1(sna tshogs): 'di ni chos gter mchog dang chos mdzad dam pa yin// sangs rgyas rigs yin 'gro ba'i bde dang skyid pa'i mdzod
28a2(sna tshogs): 'das dang ma byon phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten mgon po rnams// de dag 'di las 'khrud kyang chos dbyings zad mi 'gyur// shing dang 'bras bu me tog nags tshal ji snyed pa/
28a3(sna tshogs): de dag thams cad sa las yang dag 'byung shing 'thon// 'on kyang sa la zad pa med cing 'phel ba med// yongasu mi nyams rnam par mi rtog skye ba med// sangs rgyas
28a4(sna tshogs): sras dang nyan thos rang rgyal lha rnams dang // 'gro ba kun gyi bde skyid chos rnams ji snyed pa// de kun shes rab pha rol phyin pa mchog las byung // shes rab rnams
28a5(sna tshogs): kyang zad pa med cing 'phel ba med// sems can tha ma 'bring dang mchog gyur ji snyed pa// de kun shes rab pha rol phyin rkyen rnams tshogs no// sdug bsngal 'khrul
28a6(sna tshogs): 'khor rab tu 'byung // ma rig 'khrul 'khor 'di ni zad med 'phel ba med// ye shes tshul sgrothabs dang rtsa ba ji snyed pa// de kun shes rab pha rol phyin pa mchog
28a7(sna tshogs): las byung // rkyen rnams tshogs nas las kyi 'khrul 'khor rab tu 'byung // shes rab pha rol phyin pa bzang med 'phel ba med// byang chub sems dpa' gang
28a8(sna tshogs): pa mchog las byung //
28b1(sna tshogs): zhig rten cing 'brel 'byung la// skye med zag pa med par shes rab shing shes te// nyi ma sprin med 'od zer 'phro bas mun gsal ltar// ma rig thibs po bcom
28b2(sna tshogs): nas rang byung thob par 'gyur// mthu chen ldan rnams bsam gtan bzhis kyang gnas byed la// rten par byed pa ma yin gnas par byed pa med// 'on kyang bsam
28b3(sna tshogs): gtan yan lag bcas pa bzhi po 'di// byang chub dam pa mchog thob pa yi rten du 'gyur// shes rab mchog thob bsam gtan dag la gnas pa ni// tshad med
28b4(sna tshogs): ting 'dzin dam pa bzhi yang nyam su myong // bsam gtan drug byang chub dam pa mchog la phan// byang chub sems dpa' zag pa zad phyir slob pa min// 'di ni yon
28b5(sna tshogs): tan rdzogs pa'i ngo mtshar rmad byung ste// bsam gtan ting 'dzin la gnas nas mtshan ma med// de la gnas rnams gal te lus ni zhig gyur na// bsam pa ji bzhin
28b6(sna tshogs): 'dod pa'i khamasu yang skye'o// dper na 'dzam gling mi zhig sngon chad lha yul gyi// lha yi grong khyer mchog tu ma phyin phyis song ste// de na yongasu dga' ba'i yul de rnams
28b7(sna tshogs): mthong nas// phyir 'dir 'ongs par gyur na chags par mi byed ltar// de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' yon tan mchog 'chang ba// rnal 'byor brtson te bsam gtan
29a1(sna tshogs): ting 'dzin la gnas nas// phyir yang 'dod pa'i khams su gnas te chags pa med// chu yi pad ma bzhin du
29a2(sna tshogs): byis pa'i chos mi gnas// bdag nyid chen pos sems can yongasu smin bya dang // zhing spyod pha rol phyin rdzogs don byed kho nar zad// byang chub yon tan pha rol phyin
29a3(sna tshogs): nyams 'gyur 'ong zhes// gzugs med khamasu skye ba don gnyer mi byed pa// dper na mi zhig rin chen gter ni rnyed gyur nas// de la 'dod pa'i blo ni skyed par ma
29a4(sna tshogs): byas la// des kyang dus gzhan zhig na de dag yongs blangs shing // blangs nas khyim du song ste chags par mi byed ltar// de bzhin byang chub sems dpa'
29a5(sna tshogs): mkhas pa dga' ba dang // bde sbyin bsam gtan ting 'dzin zhi ba bzhi thob nas// bsam gtan bde ldan bsam gtan ting 'dzin thob btang ste// 'gro la
29a6(sna tshogs): snying rtser ldan pa'i phyir yang 'dod khams 'jug/ gal te byang chub sems dpa' ting 'dzin bsam gtan gnas// dgra bcom rang rgyal theg par 'dod pa'i
29a7(sna tshogs): blo bskyed na// mnyam par ma gzhag rgod sems g.yengs gyur pa ste// sangs rgyas yon tan yongs nyams mnyan pagu zhig bzhin// gzhan yang gzugs dang
29b1(sna tshogs): sgra dang de bzhin dri dang ro// reg dang 'dod yon lnga la mngon par brtson gyur kyang // dgra bcom rang rgyal theg bral byang chub sems dga' na// dpe' bo rtag tu ma
29b2(sna tshogs): bzhag yin par shes par bya// sems can gang zag gzhan phyir sems dpa' rnams dag pa// brtson 'grus pha rol phyin la mngon brtson rnam par spyod// dper na
29b3(sna tshogs): bran mo chu chun dbang med rje bo'i dbang // de bzhin dpa' rnams sems can kun gyi dbang gi 'gro// spo ba byas sam 'on te rtag tu rdeg kyang rung // bran mo rje bo la ni zlos
29b4(sna tshogs): tshig mi smra yi// 'di yis bdag ni bsad par 'gyur du 'ong snyam nas// shin tu skrag pa'i yid kyis 'jigs bcas zil gyis gnon// de bzhin byang chub ched du byang chu
29b5(sna tshogs): mchog zhags pa/ sangs rgyas yon tan 'thob cing yon tan rdzogs par 'gyur// rtsa dang shing las me byung bas ni de nyid sreg/ bdag gi bde ba btang nas re med
29b6(sna tshogs): sems nad kyi dom pa nyin mtshan mngon par brtson// bu gcig pa la mini rim 'gro byed pa ltar// bsam pa zag pas rnam par skyo med gnas par gyis// byang chub
29b7(sna tshogs): sems dpa' gang zhig yun rings 'khor 'dod cing // sems can don dang ldan zhing brtson pa'i rnal 'byor pa// yongs skyo ba'i blo ni rdul tsam skyed mi byed/
29b8(sna tshogs): 'gro kun la zar gyur bzhin du gnas par bya//
30a1(sna tshogs): de na brtson 'grus pha rol phyin ldan g.yel ba med// byang chub sems dpa' mi mkhas bskal pa bye ba bgrang
30a2(sna tshogs): gal te ring bar 'du shes sdug bsngal byang chub sgrub// yang dag chos sgrub byed che yun reng sdug bsngal 'gyur// de nas brtson 'grus pha rol byin nyams le lo can/
30a3(sna tshogs): byang chub ba chog tu sems bskyed dang po nas bzung ste/ byang chub bla na me de 'thob par 'gyur gyi dbang // nyin mtshan cig tsam du ni yid la sems byed na// mkhas
30a4(sna tshogs): pa gsal bas brtson 'grus rtsams par rig par bya// gal te 'ga' zhig 'di skad ri rab ri ba shig pa'i// rjes la byang chub mchog tho ba 'gyur zhes smra ba las/
30a5(sna tshogs): ci ste skyo ba'i yid skye chad kyang sems byed na// bdag tu 'du shes gnas pas le lor gyur pa ste// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid las rang 'gyur gnams bzhin// gal
30a6(sna tshogs): te gang che lus dang sems dang sems can 'du shes med// 'du shes rnam par log nas gnyis su med chos spyod// 'di ni byang chub zhi pa mi mnyams mchog 'dod pa'i
30a7(sna tshogs): brtson 'grus pha rol phyin ces phan pa mdzad pas gsungs// gal te gzhan las ngan brjod tshig rtsub thos gyur na// bdag bde yin zhes byang chub sems dpa'
30b1(sna tshogs): mkhas pa dga'// su smra sus thob gang gis gang zhig gang gi phyir// bzod pa'i pha rol phyin mchog ldan pa mdzad pa yin// byang chub sems dpa' gang zhig bzod
30b2(sna tshogs): pa'i legs chos ldan// gang zhig stong gsum rin chen bkang ste 'jig rten mkhyen// sangs rgyas rnams dang dgra bcom rang rgyal phul byas pas// sbyin pa'i phung
30b3(sna tshogs): pos de la bsod nams char mi phod// bzod la granas pa'i lus ni yongs su dag gyur te// sum bcu rtsa gnyis mtshan dang mthu stobs pa mtha' yas// sems can
30b4(sna tshogs): rnams la chos rab stong pa sgrogs par byed// 'di ni bzod ldan de la 'gro ba dge' 'gyur mkhas// gal te sems can la laso tsan dan phur ma blangs// rab gus bya
30b5(sna tshogs): chub sems dpa' lin nyug byed la/ gzhan zhig me 'dag mgo la mthor byed gnyis la// de yis mnyam zhing snyoms pa'i yid ni bskyed par bya// byang chub sem
30b6(sna tshogs): dpa' mkhas pas de ltar bzod byas nas// sems bskyed de ni byang chub mchog tu yongs bsngo na// dpa' bo 'jig rten kun la bzod pas dgra bcom dang /
30b7(sna tshogs): rang rgyal sems can khams kyi ji snyed zil gyis gnon// bzod byed 'di snyam du yang sems ni bskyed byed ste// sems dmyal dud 'gro gshin rje'i 'jig rten sdug
31a1(sna tshogs): / bsngal papa/ 'dod pa'i yon tan rgya yis gnon mong na/ byang chub ched duci phyir nga bzod ma bya ste// sdug
31a2(sna tshogs): dbyigs mtshon dang bsad dang bcing dang brdegs pa dang // mgo gcod pa dang rna ba rkang lag snga gcod dang // 'jig rten sdug bsngal ji snyed bdag gris bzod snyam
31a3(sna tshogs): ba/ byang chub sems dpa' bzod pa'i pha rol phyin la gnas// tshul khrims kyis ri zhi ba 'dod rnams 'phags par 'gyur// stobs bcu'i spyod yul gnas
31a4(sna tshogs): shing tshul khrims nyams pa med// sdom pa'i bya ba ji snyed kun gyi rjes su 'jug/ sems can rnams la phan phyir de yang byang chub bsngo// gal te rang rgyal dgra
31a5(sna tshogs): bcom byang chub reg 'dod ni// tshul khrims 'chal cing mi mkhas de bzhin spyod pa nyams// ci ste bang chu ba zhi ba mchog tu yongs bsngo na// 'dod yon brtson yang
31a6(sna tshogs): tshul khrims pha rol phyin la gnas// chos gang nges pa'i byang chub yon tan 'byung 'gyur ba// do ni yon tan chos ldan rnams kyi tshul khrims don// chos gang phan
31a7(sna tshogs): byed rnams kyi byang chub yongs nyams pa// de ni dul khrims 'chal ces rnam par 'dren pas gsungs// gal te byang chub sems dpa' 'dod yon lnga spyod kyang
31b1(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas chos dang 'phags pa'i dge 'dun skyabs song ste// sangs rgyas 'grub bya snyam du kun mkhyen yid byed na// mkhas pa tshul khrims pha rol phyin gnas
31b2(sna tshogs): rig par bya// gal te bskal pa bye bar dge ba'i las lam nu// spyod kyang rang rgyal dgra bcom nyid la 'dod skyed na// de tshe tshul khrims skyor byung tshul khrims
31b3(sna tshogs): nyams pa yin// sems bskyed de ni blam+ba pas kyang ni shin tu lci// tshul khrims bsrung zhing byang chub sems mchog tu yongs bsngol// de yis rlom sems med cing
31b4(sna tshogs): dga' bstod mi byed la// de yi 'du shes sems can 'du shes yongs su spangs// byang chub sems dpa' tshul khrims pha rol phyin gnas brjod// gal te byang chub
31b5(sna tshogs): sems dpa' rgyal ba'i lam spyod pa// sems can 'di dag khrims ldan 'di dag khrims 'tshal ces// sna tshogs 'du shes zhugs pa shin tu tshul khrims 'tshal/

31b7(sna tshogs): yod// gang la sdom dang sdom pa ma yin rlob sems med// 'di ni tshul khrims sdom par 'dren pas gsungs// sems can dag pa gang zhig de ltar khrims ldan pa
32a1(sna tshogs): sdug dang mi sdug kun la lta ba med pa yin// mgo dang rkang lag gtong zhing zhum pa'i sems kyang med/

32a3(sna tshogs): de tshe phyi rol dngos po gtong pa spos ci dgos// gal te ser sna byed pa de ni gnas med do// bdag tu 'du shes dngos la bdag gir 'dzin pas chags/ blun po rnams la
32a4(sna tshogs): gtong ba'i blo lhag la yod/ ser sna can ni yi dgas gnas su skye bar 'gyur/ ci ste mir skyes na yang de tshe dbul por 'gyur// de tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems can
32a5(sna tshogs): dbul shes nas// gtong la mos par 'gyur zhing rtag tu lhug par gtong // gling bzhi legs par brgyan pa'i tshil ma'i thal ba 'dra// byin na dga' bar 'gyur gyi gling thob
32a6(sna tshogs): de lta min// byang chub sems dpa' mkhas pa gsal bsrid gsum gyi// sems can ji snyed de dag kun la sbyin pa 'di// byin par gyur cig snyam du bsams nas
32a7(sna tshogs): sbyin byin la// de yang 'gro ba'i don du byang chub mchog tu sngo/ sbyin pa byin nas dngos la chags par byed pa med// de ni nam du'ang rnam par smin la ra ba med/
32b1(sna tshogs): de ltar gtong ba mkhas pa thams cad gtong ba ste// chung ngu gtong la mang po dpag tu med par 'gyur// srid pa gsum ni sems can ma lus ji snyed pa// yongasu brtag
32b2(sna tshogs): pa bzung ste de dag thams cad kyis// 'jig rten mkhyen pa sangs rgyas rang rgyal dgra bcom la// bskal pa mtha' yas sprin byin nyan thos legs tshol na// byang chub

32b7(sna tshogs): yid btags 'gro ba gcod// dbul pad+ma ni de bzhin nyon mongs thams cad gcod// spyod che longs spyod mtha' yas rgyas pa thob par 'gyur// sbyin pas sdug bsngal
33a1(sna tshogs): / gyur ba'i sems can yongs srir byed// khrims kyis dung 'gro'i 'gro ba du ma'i ngo ba dag 'i khom brgyang grong de yis ngal bsdug

33a3(sna tshogs): 'gyur// ye shes mtha' yas rgyal ba'i bang mdzod rnyed par 'gyur// bsam gtan gyi ni 'dod pa'i yon tan spang ba 'dor// rig dang mngon par shes dang ting 'dzin mngon par/

33a6(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas rgyu dang chos kyi rgyud kyang yongasu 'dzin// de bzhin dge 'dun rgyud dang chos kun yongasu rdzogs// 'gro ba'i nang gso mdzad pa sman pa'i mchog gyur pas/
33a7(sna tshogs): shes rab bstan pa byang chub lam ldan 'di gsungs te// ming ni yon ta na rin chen sdud pa byang chub lam// la ma 'di sems can kun gyis thob par bya phyir bshad//
33b1(sna tshogs): 'phags pa shes rab pha rol tu phyin pa sdud pa tshigs su bcad pa rdzogs s+ho// / rgya gar gyi mkhan po byid+ya.a ka ra sing hA dang // dan shi la dang // zhu chen gyi lo tsA
33b2(sna tshogs): ban de dpal rtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa// brgya dpe la bltas nas sho lo ka bris// sum brgya dang brgyad gda'o// bod la sum brgya dang drug brda
33b3(sna tshogs): na mo b+ha ga wa t+yai ar+ya pradz+nyA pa ra mi ta ya~M// tad+yathA// oM mu ne rnga me/ saM gra h+nadza rme// a nu gra ha rdarme/ sa ta a nu gra ha rda rje// bai sha wa Na pa ri wa ra tid+harme/ sarbaka
33b4(sna tshogs): ba ri pra pa Na d+harme// sa man+ta e nu pa ri brti dza rme swAhA// oM prar+d+ha shru ti s+thi ti bi dza yod+d+hi// d+hA ra Ni ye swA hA// 'di bzung bas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa bzung
33b5(sna tshogs): bar 'gyur ro// 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la phyag 'tshal lo// sher snying saM s+thi te ne// na mo b+ha ga wa t+yai Ar+ya pradz+nyA pA ra ma tA yi// e waM ma ya shru tas+the smi nas
33b6(sna tshogs): ma ye// drug wAn ra da kri he// bi bar tes ma kr-i d+ha ku Te// bar bte/ ma hA \u0f7f prIk+Sha si ste nasar d+ha ma ma hA hAH bo d+his twas sbyin// te me ba'u bran/ ten 'khru bran/
33b7(sna tshogs): sa ma yin// b+hag zan// ga~M b+hI ra bra b+ha saM na ma d+ha rme b.rA yas mA d+hi sam ban+da/ na tsas ma ye/ ar+ya lo ki te shwa ro bo d+hi sa two ma hA sa twa ga b+hi ra yaM/ pradz+nyA ba ra mai tA ya
34a1(sna tshogs): tsar+ya mes bya ba lo ka ya ti s+kha/ pany+tsa sman \u0f7f sh+yas b+ha ba shung n+ya na bya ba lo ka ya ti swa/ a tha suSh+mA sha ri bud
34a2(sna tshogs): two bud nu b+ha ba na r+ya ba lo ki te sha ram/ mahA sa ta me tad bo tsata/ i ha r+ya ba lo ki ti sha ra ku pu tri na ba kul du hi tA ba/ gaM b+ha ra yaM pradz+nyA pA ra mi ta yAM/ tsar+ya ta tse re tu ka
34a3(sna tshogs): me na ka thaM bya ba lo ka yi ta byaM/ ar+yA ba lo ki te sha ra A ha/ yaHke shI tsi shwa ri tsi bu tr-i/ ku la putwo ba ku la du hri tA bA/ gai b+hi rA yaM/ pradz+nyA pA ra mi ta yaM/ tsAr+ya
34a4(sna tshogs): tsar tu// kA ma ste ne wa bya ba lo ka yi tabyaM/ pany+tsa skan d+ha/ swe b+ha ba shUn+ya i ti bya lo ka yi ta byaM/ ru paM shun+ya ti/ be na rU pa ta pri thi ka shUn+ya t+ya yA ne pr-i tha ka ru paM/ a~M
34a5(sna tshogs): tha ba da na saM dz+nyA saM skar/ bi dz+nyA nA ni shA n+ya ni/ e waM shA ri pu tra sa d+harma/ shU n+yaH/ a lak+Sha NA/ a nud bin na/ a nid rud d+ha/ a ma la/ bi ma la/ a nu na
34a6(sna tshogs): a saM pur kye ta smad tA tsau shA r-i pu tra/ shAn+yat+na yo/ nA ru baM/ na bod na/ nas dz+nyA/ nas skar/ na badz+nyAn/ nanak+ta/ na shrot+tAM/ nan/ ni hA/
34a7(sna tshogs): na ka yo// nam na/ na ru baM/ na shab do/ nagani // nar so// na s+phar sho// na d+hamaM/ nanak+Sha ra d+ha tu/ ya bin na mo na/ d+ha tu ra na ma no// bidz+nyA nadA tu ra ni bi d+yak+Sha ye
34b1(sna tshogs): ya ba na na dza ra ma raH/ nadzar ma ranak+Sha lo// nadu/ khaM nas mu 'ang yo ni ni ro rnon mAr g+hon dz+nyA na/ na pra pa ti/ na pra ba ti/ karba/ sha ri putA/ a pra paNI/
34b2(sna tshogs): tad b+ho d+hi satwa/ pradz+nyA pa ra mi tA ma shwa t+yai ba ha ran ti/ tsit+ta ta ram/ ba NaM mA tA trad/ a tra s+thA/ bi par+yas ti kran tA ni ra pA Na pra pa ta/ trad+ba bya ba s+thi ti/ sarba bud d+hi ribi/
34b3(sna tshogs): badz+nyA pA ra mi tA mA shri t+yai nud tA ra ma sa myags b+ho d+hi ma b+hi saM bud d+ha/ ta smad ta ra he dz+nyA ta byaM pradz+nyA pA re mi tA maM traM/ ma hA bi d+ye man ta/ a nud ta ro man tra/ a sa ma sa mo man

125b5(sna tshogs): mtshan nyid med pa de'i phyir/ de dag la chags pa med do// des ni chos thams cad la chags pa med pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya ste/ ji skad du brjod

126a1(sna tshogs): pa'i phyir chags pa med pa'i mtshan nyid do// sha ri'i bu chos gang chags pa med pa'i mtshan nyid kyi chos gang
126a2(sna tshogs): yin pa pa de ni mthong ba cir yang nye bar gnas pa ma yin shing / mi mthong ba yang ma yin mod kyi// 'on kyang seMsmra rnams la chags pa med pa'i mtshan nyid ces
126a3(sna tshogs): bstan par byas so// sha ri'i bu kan nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid gang yin pa de ni med pa ste/ kun nas nyon mongs de ni mtshan nyid kyis nye bar gnas pa ma yin gyi
126a4(sna tshogs): sha ri'i bu kun nas nyon mongs pa ni byin ci log gis nye bar gnas pa'o// phyin ci log gang yin pa de ni mtshan nyid med pa'o// gang mtshan nyid med pa de tha snyad kyis
126a5(sna tshogs): kyang mtshan nyid med de/ de mtshan nyid med pa kho na'o// sha ri'i bu rnam par byang ba gang yin pa de yang mtshan nyid med pa'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sha ri'i bu kun nas nyon mo/
126a6(sna tshogs): pa nyid kyang mtshan nyid med na/ rnam par byang ba lta ci smos/ sha ri'i bu gang kun nas nyon mongs pa yongs su shes pa de ni yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin te/ de la kun nas
126a7(sna tshogs): nyon mongs pa ci yang med mod kyi/ sems can rnams ni phyin ci log pas kun nas nyon mongs pa'o// gang phyin ci log de yang dag par ma yin no// gang yang dag pa ma yin pa de
126b1(sna tshogs): yang dag pa yongs su grub pa 'am/ mtshan sbed do// sha ra dwa ti'i bu gang de ltar shes pa de ni rnam par byang ba zhes bya'o// kun nas nyon mongs pa nyid kyang mtshan nyid med na/
126b2(sna tshogs): rnam par byang ba lta ci smos/ sha rar dwa ti'i bu 'di lta ste/ kun nas nyon mongs pa 'am/ rnam par byang ba'i chos 'di gnyis ni mtshan nyid med cing yongs su ma grub pa'o//
126b3(sna tshogs): sha ri'i bu chos thams cad ni mtshan nyid med cing yongs su ma grub pa ste/ da ni chags pa med pa zhes bya'o// chos thams cad chags pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya ba ni chos thams
126b4(sna tshogs): cad chags pa med pa yin na/ sha ri'i bu byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad ni chags pa med pa la chags so// sha ri'i bu 'di ni chos thams cad la chags pa med pa'i mtshan
126b5(sna tshogs): nyid de/ ye shes kyi spyod yul zhes bstan to// sha ri'i bu 'di ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i yul lo// chags pa med pa'i mtshan nyid ye shes kyi spyod yul ni shes
126b6(sna tshogs): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ste/ de'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i spyod yul mtha' yas zhes bya'o// gang chags pa med pa de'i yul dang / spyod yul mtha' yas so//
126b7(sna tshogs): sha ri'i bu spyod yul zhes bya ba de ni spyod yul med pa'i tshig bla dgas so// sha ri'i bu shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni spyod yul bstan pa'i mtshan nyid kyis bya ba yin no//
127a1(sna tshogs): shA ri'i bu yul zhes bya ba'i de ni chos thams cad yul med pa'o// de ni yang dag pa ji lta ba nyid dang / ji lta ba bzhin no//

127a6(sna tshogs): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyir mi ldog pa/ lta ba phun tshogs pa'i gang zag phyir mi ldog pa rnams ma gtogs par grogs gzhan gang yang med de/
127a7(sna tshogs): lta ba phun sum tshogs pa chos 'di la sprod pa'i de dag kyang tha tshom du 'gyur ro// sha ri'i bu byang chub sems dpa' the tshom du med pa/ lus mngon sum du
127b1(sna tshogs): gyur pa rnams chos 'di la bzod pa thob par 'gyur gyi/ sha ri'i bu byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams ni ma yin no// sha ri'i bu shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bstan pa/
127b2(sna tshogs): 'di ni/ dman pa la mos pa'i sems can rnams kyi lag tu 'gro bar mi 'gyur gyi/ shA ri'i bu shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bstan pa 'di ni sems can gang dag dge
127b3(sna tshogs): ba'i rtsa ba yongs su dag pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas mang po la bsnyen bkur byas pa de dag gi lag tu 'gro bar 'gyur ro// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bstan
127b4(sna tshogs): pa 'di ni/ sems can gang dag dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa/ bsam pa gre ba/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams lhag par bya ba byas pa/ byang chub kyi phyir sa
127b5(sna tshogs): bon bskyed pa/ sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la zhugs pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang nye bar bzhag pa/ tshul bzhin du kun 'dri ba de dag gi lag tu
127b6(sna tshogs): 'gro bar 'gyur ro// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bstan pa 'di ni gang dag bzod pa thob pa dang nye bar 'gyur ba dang / bzod pa de dag gi lag tu 'gro bar
127b7(sna tshogs): 'gyur ro// gang dag lung bstan pa de dag kyang myur du bla na med pa dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur te/ smon lam/

128b1(sna tshogs): dang / dbang po phyal bar mi bya'o// sha ri'i bu gang dag dge ba'i rtsa ba byas pa dag kyang mi slu'o// byang chub sems dpas chos 'di rnyed nas bag yod pa dang / brtson

128b6(sna tshogs): de dag gis 'di lta bu'i chos 'di thos pa ma yin no// sha ri'i bu thos zhes bya ba de ni yang dag pa'i nan tan gyi tshig bla dgas te/ le lo'i nan tan gi ni ma yin no//
128b7(sna tshogs): sha ri'i bu log par zhugs pas ni chos 'di thos par mi 'gyur ro// sha ri'i bu thos nas khyed don la mkhas shing nan tan gyis gnas par bya'o// sha ri'i bu log par zhugs

290b3(sna tshogs): dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das yul ma ga ta dgon par chos kyi snying por bzhugs te/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing tshad med grangs med pa nas 'dus pa'i byang chub sems
290b4(sna tshogs): dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing rdul phra mo dang mnyam pa dang thabs gcigo// thams cad kyang kun tu bzang po'i smon lam la mnga' brnyes pa spyod pa la gnas pa'o// de nas byang chub sems
290b5(sna tshogs): dpa' kun tu bzang pos chos thams cad rnams par mi rtog pa bstan pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhug so// tingange 'dzin de'i mthus 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi
290b6(sna tshogs): zhing gi rdul phra mo dang mnyam pa thams cad g.yos so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la phyag gi dbu la reg par gyur to// de ltar reg pas sangs
290b7(sna tshogs): rgyas kyi zhing rnams kyang rab tu g.yos par gyur/ lha rnams kyis mthun par tshig su bcasde pas stod pa/ 'jig rten sgro na ma lha ma'i dpe las 'das/ yon tan rgya mtsho lta bur pha rol phyin//
291a1(sna tshogs): @srid pa'i mtsho las 'gro ba khyod kyis sgrol/ ded dpon khyod kyis rab tu bskyab par gsol/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos/
291a2(sna tshogs): bcom ldan 'das la 'dis skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ji ltar bslab par bya ba'i don shes rab dang 'dra ba dang / shes rab yin pa le bslab par bya/ bcom ldan 'das
291a3(sna tshogs): kyis bka' stsal pa/ kun tu bzang po shes rab dang 'dra ba ni/ 'jig rten tshogs kyi lam pa rnams kyi shes rab gang yin pa'o// shes rab yin pa ni sa dang po yan chad kyi shes rab gang
291a4(sna tshogs): yin pa'o// bcos ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po dang / lha dang mir bcas pa'i 'jig rten yi rangs te/ bcom ldan

291b1(sna tshogs): 'dug bstan las langs nas bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ji ltar bslab par bgyi/

291b3(sna tshogs): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// gzhan yang gzugs la sogs pa'i chos thams cad rang bzhin ma mchis pa dang / mtshan ma ma mchis pa dang / dngos
291b4(sna tshogs): po dang bral ba dang / mi dmigs pas na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// nang stong pa nyid nas dngos po med pa stong pa nyid kyi phyir na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
291b5(sna tshogs): byin/ pa la bslab par bya'o// lag na rdo rje shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di ni dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yum ste/ rig pa chen po'i sngags 'di'i tshig ni 'di
291b6(sna tshogs): dag go/ tad+ya thA/ oM mu ni mu ni/ ma hA mu na ye swA hA/ su zhig shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di 'dzin par byed na/ dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos rnams bzung
291b7(sna tshogs): bar 'gyur ro// de skye ba dran par 'gyur ro// mi khom pa thams cad spangs par 'gyur ro// bsod nams kyi 'bras bu tshad med pa thob par 'gyur ro//
292a1(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang dus rtag tu 'grogs par 'gyur ro// byang chub kyi sems dang ldan par 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das
292a2(sna tshogs): kyis de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' phyag na rdo rje dang / lha dang mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yi rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
292a3(sna tshogs): gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lag na rdo rje'i mdo// theg pa chen po rdzog s+ho/ @#// rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya pradz+nyA pA/
292a4(sna tshogs): ra mi tA badz+ra ke tu ma hA yA na sU tra/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi mdo theg pa chen po// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la
292a5(sna tshogs): phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das rgyal po'i khab na bzhugs te/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor dang thabs gcig go// de nas de'i
292a6(sna tshogs): tshe'akhor der byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje rgyal mtshan 'dug pa de stan las langs te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das chos gang dang ldan na shes rab
292a7(sna tshogs): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan chos rnam pa bzhi dang ldan na ste/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad stong pa nyid du/
292b1(sna tshogs): mngon pa dang / 'dus byas thams cad mi rtag pa dang / sdug bsngal bar shes pa dang spros pa thams cad dang bral ba'i chos nyid du ldan pa dang / thams cad mi rtog mi dmigs par
292b2(sna tshogs): bsgom pa'o// gzhan yang chos rnam bzhi dang ldan na shes rab skye ba'i rgyu ste/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dang po gang zag chos spro ba'i mkhan po rten pa dang / gnyis pa de'i dam
292b3(sna tshogs): pa'i chos nyan pa dang / gsum pa don la 'jug cing sems pa dang / bzhi pa bzhan la tshul bzhin du ston par mos pa ste/ 'di ni shes rab skye ba'i rgyu'o// rigs kyi bu

292b5(sna tshogs): dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / ma bcings pa dang / ma grol ba dang / snang ba med pa dang / mun pa med pa'i rang bzhin du shes par bya'o// de lta bas na byang chub sems dpa'
292b6(sna tshogs): rnams kyis shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// chos thams cad skye ba med pa dang / gnas pa med pa'i tshul gyis shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par
